# <a name="exfat-file-system-specification"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-103">exFAT 檔案系統規格</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-103">exFAT file system specification</span></span>

## <a name="1-introduction"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-104">1 簡介</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-104">1 Introduction</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-105">ExFAT 檔案系統是 FAT32 在 FAT 檔案系統中的後續版本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-105">The exFAT file system is the successor to FAT32 in the FAT family of file systems.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-106">此規格描述 exFAT 檔案系統，並提供執行 exFAT 檔案系統所需的所有資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-106">This specification describes the exFAT file system and provides all the information necessary for implementing the exFAT file system.</span></span>

### <a name="11-design-goals"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-107">1.1 設計目標</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-107">1.1 Design Goals</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-108">ExFAT 檔案系統有三個集中設計目標 (請參閱以下) 的清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-108">The exFAT file system has three central design goals (see list below).</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-109">*保留以 FAT 為基礎之檔案系統的簡潔性。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-109">*Retain the simplicity of FAT-based file systems.*</span></span>

   > <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-110">FAT 型檔案系統的兩大優點是它們的相對簡單和簡化。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-110">Two of the strengths of FAT-based file systems are their relative simplicity and ease of implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-111">在其前身的精神中，實作者應該發現 exFAT 相當簡單，而且易於實行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-111">In the spirit of its predecessors, implementers should find exFAT relatively simple and easy to implement.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-112">*啟用非常大型的檔案和存放裝置。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-112">*Enable very large files and storage devices.*</span></span>

   > <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-113">ExFAT 檔案系統會使用64位來描述檔案大小，進而啟用相依于大型檔案的應用程式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-113">The exFAT file system uses 64 bits to describe file size, thereby enabling applications which depend on very large files.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-114">ExFAT 檔案系統也可讓叢集大到32MB，有效啟用極大型的儲存裝置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-114">The exFAT file system also allows for clusters as large as 32MB, effectively enabling very large storage devices.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-115">*納入擴充性以進行未來的創新。*</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-115">*Incorporate extensibility for future innovation.*</span></span>

   > <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-116">ExFAT 檔案系統將擴充性納入其設計中，讓檔案系統能夠與儲存體中的創新和使用方式的變更保持一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-116">The exFAT file system incorporates extensibility into its design, enabling the file system to keep pace with innovations in storage and changes in usage.</span></span>

### <a name="12-specific-terminology"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-117">1.2 特定術語</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-117">1.2 Specific Terminology</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-118">在此規格的內容中，特定詞彙 (請參閱 [表 1](#table-1-definition-of-terms-which-carry-very-specific-meaning)) 針對 exFAT 檔案系統的設計和執行提供特定意義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-118">In the context of this specification, certain terms (see [Table 1](#table-1-definition-of-terms-which-carry-very-specific-meaning)) carry specific meaning for the design and implementation of the exFAT file system.</span></span>

<div id="table-1-definition-of-terms-which-carry-very-specific-meaning" />

### <a name="14-default-field-and-structure-qualifiers"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-173">1.4 預設欄位和結構限定詞</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-173">1.4 Default Field and Structure Qualifiers</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-174">此規格中的欄位和結構具有下列限定詞 (請參閱以下) 的清單，除非指定其他規格的附注。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-174">Fields and structures in this specification have the following qualifiers (see list below), unless the specification notes otherwise.</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-175">未簽署</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-175">Are unsigned</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-176">使用小數點標記法來描述值，如果未另行注明則為。此規格會使用修正後字母 "h" 來表示十六進位數位，並將 Guid 括在大括弧中</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-176">Use decimal notation to describe values, where not otherwise noted; this specification uses the post-fix letter "h" to denote  hexadecimal numbers and encloses GUIDs in curly braces</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-177">以位元組由小到大格式</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-177">Are in little-endian format</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-178">字串不需要以 null 結尾的字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-178">Do not require a null-terminating character for strings</span></span>

### <a name="15-windows-ce-and-texfat"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-179">1.5 Windows CE 和 TexFAT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-179">1.5 Windows CE and TexFAT</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-180">TexFAT 是 exFAT 的延伸模組，可在基底檔案系統之上新增交易安全操作的語法。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-180">TexFAT is an extension to exFAT that adds transaction-safe operational semantics on top of the base file system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-181">Windows CE 會使用 TexFAT。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-181">TexFAT is used by Windows CE.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-182">TexFAT 需要使用兩個 FATs 和配置點陣圖，才能在交易中使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-182">TexFAT requires the use of the two FATs and allocation bitmaps for use in transactions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-183">它也會定義數個額外的結構，包括填補描述項和安全描述項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-183">It also defines several additional structures including padding descriptors and security descriptors.</span></span>

## <a name="2-volume-structure"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-184">2個磁片區結構</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-184">2 Volume Structure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-185">磁片區是儲存和取出使用者資料所需的所有檔案系統結構和資料空間的集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-185">A volume is the set of all file system structures and data space necessary to store and retrieve user data.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-186">所有 exFAT 磁片區都包含四個區域 (請參閱 [表 3](#table-3-volume-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-186">All exFAT volumes contain four regions (see [Table 3](#table-3-volume-structure)).</span></span>

<div id="table-3-volume-structure" />

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-187">**表3磁片區結構**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-187">**Table 3 Volume Structure**</span></span>

## <a name="3-main-and-backup-boot-regions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-270">3個主要和備份開機區域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-270">3 Main and Backup Boot Regions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-271">主要開機區域會提供所有必要的開機搭接接指令、識別資訊和檔案系統參數，讓執行執行下列動作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-271">The Main Boot region provides all the necessary boot-strapping instructions, identifying information, and file system parameters to enable an implementation to perform the following:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-272">從 exFAT 磁片區將電腦系統開機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-272">Boot-strap a computer system from an exFAT volume.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-273">將磁片區上的檔案系統識別為 exFAT。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-273">Identify the file system on the volume as exFAT.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-274">探索 exFAT 檔案系統結構的位置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-274">Discover the location of the exFAT file system structures.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-275">備份開機區域是主要開機區域的備份。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-275">The Backup Boot region is a backup of the Main Boot region.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-276">當主要開機區域處於不一致的狀態時，它會協助復原 exFAT 磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-276">It aids recovery of the exFAT volume in the event of the Main Boot region being in an inconsistent state.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-277">除非在罕見的情況下（例如更新開機搭接接指令），否則不應該修改備份開機區域的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-277">Except under infrequent circumstances, such as updating boot-strapping instructions, implementations should not modify the contents of the Backup Boot region.</span></span>

### <a name="31-main-and-backup-boot-sector-sub-regions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-278">3.1 主要和備份開機磁區子領域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-278">3.1 Main and Backup Boot Sector Sub-regions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-279">主要開機磁區包含搭接接自 exFAT 磁片區的開機程式碼，以及描述磁片區結構的基本 exFAT 參數， (參閱 [表 4](#table-4-main-and-backup-boot-sector-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-279">The Main Boot Sector contains code for boot-strapping from an exFAT volume and fundamental exFAT parameters which describe the volume structure (see [Table 4](#table-4-main-and-backup-boot-sector-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-280">BIOS、MBR 或其他開機搭接接代理程式可能會檢查此磁區，而且可能會載入並執行其中所包含的任何開機搭接接指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-280">BIOS, MBR, or other boot-strapping agents may inspect this sector and may load and execute any boot-strapping instructions contained therein.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-281">備份開機磁區是主要開機磁區的備份，而且具有相同的結構 (請參閱 [ [表 4](#table-4-main-and-backup-boot-sector-structure) ]) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-281">The Backup Boot Sector is a backup of the Main Boot Sector and has the same structure (see [Table 4](#table-4-main-and-backup-boot-sector-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-282">備份開機磁區可協助復原作業;但是，執行應該會將 VolumeFlags 和 PercentInUse 欄位的內容視為過時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-282">The Backup Boot Sector may aid recovery operations; however, implementations shall treat the contents of the VolumeFlags and PercentInUse fields as stale.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-283">在使用主要或備份開機磁區的內容之前，必須先驗證其各自的開機總和檢查碼，並確保其所有欄位都在有效的值範圍內，藉以驗證它們的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-283">Prior to using the contents of either the Main or Backup Boot Sector, implementations shall verify their contents by validating their respective Boot Checksum and ensuring all their fields are within their valid value range.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-284">初始格式作業將會初始化主要和備份開機磁區的內容，而執行程式可能會 (更新這些磁區，而且也應該視需要更新其各自的開機總和檢查碼) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-284">While the initial format operation will initialize the contents of both the Main and Backup Boot Sectors, implementations may update these sectors (and shall also update their respective Boot Checksum) as needed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-285">不過，執行可能會更新 VolumeFlags 或 PercentInUse 欄位，而不會更新其各自的開機總和檢查碼， (總和檢查碼明確地排除這兩個欄位) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-285">However, implementations may update either the VolumeFlags or PercentInUse fields without updating their respective Boot Checksum (the checksum specifically excludes these two fields).</span></span>

#### <a name="311-jumpboot-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-382">3.1.1 JumpBoot 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-382">3.1.1 JumpBoot Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-383">JumpBoot 欄位必須包含個人電腦中常見 Cpu 的跳躍指示，在執行時，會在執行程式碼欄位中「跳過」 CPU 來執行開機搭接接指令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-383">The JumpBoot field shall contain the jump instruction for CPUs common in personal computers, which, when executed, "jumps" the CPU to execute the boot-strapping instructions in the BootCode field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-384">此欄位的有效值是依低序位位元組至高序位位元組) EBh 76h 90h 的順序 (。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-384">The valid value for this field is (in order of low-order byte to high-order byte) EBh 76h 90h.</span></span>

#### <a name="312-filesystemname-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-385">3.1.2 FileSystemName 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-385">3.1.2 FileSystemName Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-386">FileSystemName 欄位應包含磁片區上檔案系統的名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-386">The FileSystemName field shall contain the name of the file system on the volume.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-387">此欄位的有效值為 ASCII 字元 "EXFAT"，其中包含三個尾端空白字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-387">The valid value for this field is, in ASCII characters, "EXFAT ", which includes three trailing white spaces.</span></span>

#### <a name="313-mustbezero-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-388">3.1.3 MustBeZero 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-388">3.1.3 MustBeZero Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-389">MustBeZero 欄位應該會直接對應到封裝 BIOS 參數區塊在 FAT12/16/32 磁片區上使用的位元組範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-389">The MustBeZero field shall directly correspond with the range of bytes the packed BIOS parameter block consumes on FAT12/16/32 volumes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-390">此欄位的有效值為0，這有助於防止 FAT12/16/32 的執行錯誤地裝載 exFAT 的磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-390">The valid value for this field is 0, which helps to prevent FAT12/16/32 implementations from mistakenly mounting an exFAT volume.</span></span>

#### <a name="314-partitionoffset-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-391">3.1.4 PartitionOffset 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-391">3.1.4 PartitionOffset Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-392">PartitionOffset 欄位應描述裝載指定 exFAT 磁片區之分割區的媒體相關磁區位移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-392">The PartitionOffset field shall describe the media-relative sector offset of the partition which hosts the given exFAT volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-393">此欄位使用個人電腦上的外延 INT 13h，協助搭接接從磁片區進行開機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-393">This field aids boot-strapping from the volume using extended INT 13h on personal computers.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-394">此欄位的所有可能值都是有效的;不過，值0表示實值應忽略此欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-394">All possible values for this field are valid; however, the value 0 indicates implementations shall ignore this field.</span></span>

#### <a name="315-volumelength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-395">3.1.5 VolumeLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-395">3.1.5 VolumeLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-396">VolumeLength 欄位必須描述指定之 exFAT 磁片區在磁區中的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-396">The VolumeLength field shall describe the size of the given exFAT volume in sectors.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-397">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-397">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-398">至少 2<sup>20</sup>/2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>，可確保最小的磁片區小於1mb</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-398">At least 2<sup>20</sup>/ 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>, which ensures the smallest volume is no less than 1MB</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-399">最大值為 2<sup>64</sup>-1，此欄位可描述的最大值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-399">At most 2<sup>64</sup>- 1, the largest value this field can describe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-400">但是，如果多餘空間子領域的大小為0，則此欄位的值為 ClusterHeapOffset + (2<sup>32</sup>-11) \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-400">However, if the size of the Excess Space sub-region is 0, then the value of this field is ClusterHeapOffset + (2<sup>32</sup>- 11) \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>.</span></span>

#### <a name="316-fatoffset-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-401">3.1.6 FatOffset 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-401">3.1.6 FatOffset Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-402">FatOffset 欄位應描述第一個 FAT 的磁片區相對磁區位移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-402">The FatOffset field shall describe the volume-relative sector offset of the First FAT.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-403">此欄位可讓您將第一個 FAT 對齊基礎儲存媒體的特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-403">This field enables implementations to align the First FAT to the characteristics of the underlying storage media.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-404">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-404">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-405">至少24，主要開機和備份開機區域所耗用的磁區帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-405">At least 24, which accounts for the sectors the Main Boot and Backup Boot regions consume</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-406">最多 ClusterHeapOffset- (FatLength \* NumberOfFats) ，其為叢集堆積所耗用的磁區帳戶</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-406">At most ClusterHeapOffset - (FatLength \* NumberOfFats), which accounts for the sectors the Cluster Heap consumes</span></span>

#### <a name="317-fatlength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-407">3.1.7 FatLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-407">3.1.7 FatLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-408">FatLength 欄位應描述每個 FAT 資料表的長度（以磁區為限） (磁片區最多可包含兩個 FATs) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-408">The FatLength field shall describe the length, in sectors, of each FAT table (the volume may contain up to two FATs).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-409">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-409">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-410">至少 (ClusterCount + 2) \* 2<sup>2</sup>/2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>進位至最接近的整數，以確保每個 FAT 都有足夠的空間來描述叢集堆積中的所有群集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-410">At least (ClusterCount + 2) \* 2<sup>2</sup>/ 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>rounded up to the nearest integer, which ensures each FAT has sufficient  space for describing all the clusters in the Cluster Heap</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-411">最多 (ClusterHeapOffset FatOffset) /NumberOfFats 四捨五入至最接近的整數，以確保 FATs 存在於叢集堆積之前</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-411">At most (ClusterHeapOffset - FatOffset) / NumberOfFats rounded down to the nearest integer, which ensures the FATs exist before the  Cluster Heap</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-412">這個欄位可能會包含超出其下限 (的值，如上面所述) 若要啟用第二個 FAT （如果有的話）也會對齊基礎儲存體媒體的特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-412">This field may contain a value in excess of its lower bound (as described above) to enable the Second FAT, if present, to also be aligned to the characteristics of the underlying storage media.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-413">未定義空間的內容，超過 FAT 本身需要的內容（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-413">The contents of the space which exceeds what the FAT itself requires, if any, are undefined.</span></span>

#### <a name="318-clusterheapoffset-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-414">3.1.8 ClusterHeapOffset 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-414">3.1.8 ClusterHeapOffset Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-415">ClusterHeapOffset 欄位應描述叢集堆積的磁片區相對磁區位移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-415">The ClusterHeapOffset field shall describe the volume-relative sector offset of the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-416">此欄位可讓您將叢集堆積對齊基礎儲存媒體的特性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-416">This field enables implementations to align the Cluster Heap to the characteristics of the underlying storage media.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-417">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-417">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-418">至少 FatOffset + FatLength \* NumberOfFats，以考慮上述所有區域所耗用的磁區</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-418">At least FatOffset + FatLength \* NumberOfFats, to account for the sectors all the preceding regions consume</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-419">最多2個<sup>32</sup>-1 或 VolumeLength- (ClusterCount \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>) ，以較少的計算</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-419">At most 2<sup>32</sup>- 1 or VolumeLength - (ClusterCount \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>), whichever calculation is less</span></span>

#### <a name="319-clustercount-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-420">3.1.9 ClusterCount 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-420">3.1.9 ClusterCount Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-421">ClusterCount 欄位應描述叢集堆積包含的叢集數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-421">The ClusterCount field shall describe the number of clusters the Cluster Heap contains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-422">此欄位的有效值應為下列較小的值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-422">The valid value for this field shall be the lesser of the following:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-423"> (VolumeLength-ClusterHeapOffset) /2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>四捨五入到最接近的整數，也就是叢集堆積和磁片區結尾之間可容納的叢集數目</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-423">(VolumeLength - ClusterHeapOffset) / 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>rounded down to the nearest integer, which is exactly the number of clusters which can fit between the beginning of the Cluster Heap and the end of the volume</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-424">2<sup>32</sup>-11，也就是 FAT 可以描述的叢集數目上限</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-424">2<sup>32</sup>- 11, which is the maximum number of clusters a FAT can describe</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-425">ClusterCount 欄位的值會決定 FAT 的大小下限。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-425">The value of the ClusterCount field determines the minimum size of a FAT.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-426">為了避免極度龐大的 FATs，可透過 [SectorsPerClusterShift] 欄位) 增加叢集大小 (，藉以控制叢集中的叢集數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-426">To avoid extremely large FATs, implementations can control the number of clusters in the Cluster Heap by increasing the cluster size (via the SectorsPerClusterShift field).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-427">此規格建議在叢集堆積中不超過2個<sup>24</sup>-2 的叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-427">This specification recommends no more than 2<sup>24</sup>- 2 clusters in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-428">不過，在叢集中，執行應該能夠處理最多有2個<sup>32</sup>-11 個叢集的磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-428">However, implementations shall be able to handle volumes with up to 2<sup>32</sup>- 11 clusters in the Cluster Heap.</span></span>

#### <a name="3110-firstclusterofrootdirectory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-429">3.1.10 FirstClusterOfRootDirectory 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-429">3.1.10 FirstClusterOfRootDirectory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-430">FirstClusterOfRootDirectory 欄位必須包含根目錄第一個叢集的叢集索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-430">The FirstClusterOfRootDirectory field shall contain the cluster index of the first cluster of the root directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-431">當配置點陣圖和向上案例資料表耗用叢集之後，執行的每一項工作都應該盡力將根目錄的第一個叢集放在第一個非錯誤的叢集中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-431">Implementations should make every effort to place the first cluster of the root directory in the first non-bad cluster after the clusters the Allocation Bitmap and Up-case Table consume.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-432">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-432">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-433">至少2個叢集堆積中第一個叢集的索引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-433">At least 2, the index of the first cluster in the Cluster Heap</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-434">最多 ClusterCount + 1，也就是叢集堆積中最後一個叢集的索引</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-434">At most ClusterCount + 1, the index of the last cluster in the Cluster Heap</span></span>

#### <a name="3111-volumeserialnumber-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-435">3.1.11 VolumeSerialNumber 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-435">3.1.11 VolumeSerialNumber Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-436">VolumeSerialNumber 欄位必須包含唯一的序號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-436">The VolumeSerialNumber field shall contain a unique serial number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-437">這可協助您區分不同的 exFAT 磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-437">This assists implementations to distinguish among different exFAT volumes.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-438">執行程式應結合 exFAT 磁片區格式化的日期和時間，以產生序號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-438">Implementations should generate the serial number by combining the date and time of formatting the exFAT volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-439">結合日期和時間以形成序號的機制是實特定的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-439">The mechanism for combining date and time to form a serial number is implementation-specific.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-440">此欄位的所有可能值都是有效的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-440">All possible values for this field are valid.</span></span>

#### <a name="3112-filesystemrevision-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-441">3.1.12 FileSystemRevision 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-441">3.1.12 FileSystemRevision Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-442">FileSystemRevision 欄位必須描述指定磁片區上 exFAT 結構的主要和次要修訂編號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-442">The FileSystemRevision field shall describe the major and minor revision numbers of the exFAT structures on the given volume.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-443">高序位位元組是主要修訂編號，低序位位元組是次要修訂編號。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-443">The high-order byte is the major revision number and the low-order byte is the minor revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-444">例如，如果高序位位元組包含值01h，而且低序位位元組包含值05h，則 FileSystemRevision 欄位會描述修訂編號1.05。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-444">For example, if the high-order byte contains the value 01h and if the low-order byte contains the value 05h, then the FileSystemRevision field describes the revision number 1.05.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-445">同樣地，如果高序位位元組包含值0Ah，且低序位位元組包含值0Fh，則 FileSystemRevision 欄位會描述修訂編號10.15。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-445">Likewise, if the high-order byte contains the value 0Ah and if the low-order byte contains the value 0Fh, then the FileSystemRevision field describes the revision number 10.15.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-446">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-446">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-447">低序位位元組至少為0，高序位位元組為1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-447">At least 0 for the low-order byte and 1 for the high-order byte</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-448">高序位位元組的低序位位元組和99最多99</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-448">At most 99 for the low-order byte and 99 for the high-order byte</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-449">此規格所描述的 exFAT 修訂編號為1.00。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-449">The revision number of exFAT this specification describes is 1.00.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-450">此規格的執行應該裝載任何具有主要修訂編號1的 exFAT 磁片區，而且不應該掛接任何其他主要修訂編號的 exFAT 磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-450">Implementations of this specification should mount any exFAT volume with major revision number 1 and shall not mount any exFAT volume with any other major revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-451">執行作業應接受次要修訂編號，且不會執行作業或建立任何未在指定的次要修訂編號的對應規格中描述的檔案系統結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-451">Implementations shall honor the minor revision number and shall not perform operations or create any file system structures not described in the given minor revision number's corresponding specification.</span></span>

#### <a name="3113-volumeflags-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-452">3.1.13 VolumeFlags 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-452">3.1.13 VolumeFlags Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-453">VolumeFlags 欄位必須包含旗標，指出 exFAT 磁片區上各種檔案系統結構的狀態 (參閱 [表 5](#table-5-volumeflags-field-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-453">The VolumeFlags field shall contain flags which indicate the status of various file system structures on the exFAT volume (see [Table 5](#table-5-volumeflags-field-structure)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-454">在計算其各自的主要開機或備份開機區域總和檢查碼時，不應包含此欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-454">Implementations shall not include this field when computing its respective Main Boot or Backup Boot region checksum.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-455">參考備份開機磁區時，執行應該會將此欄位視為過時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-455">When referring to the Backup Boot Sector, implementations shall treat this field as stale.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-456">**表 5 VolumeFlags 欄位結構**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-456">**Table 5 VolumeFlags Field Structure**</span></span>

##### <a name="31131-activefat-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-483">3.1.13.1 ActiveFat 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-483">3.1.13.1 ActiveFat Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-484">ActiveFat 欄位應該會說明哪些 FAT 和配置點陣圖是作用中的 (而實作為應使用) ，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-484">The ActiveFat field shall describe which FAT and Allocation Bitmap are active (and implementations shall use), as follows:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-485">0，表示第一個 FAT 和第一個配置點陣圖為作用中</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-485">0, which means the First FAT and First Allocation Bitmap are active</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-486">1，這表示第二個 FAT 和第二個配置點陣圖為使用中，而且只有在 NumberOfFats 欄位包含值2時，才可能使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-486">1, which means the Second FAT and Second Allocation Bitmap are active and is possible only when the NumberOfFats field contains the value 2</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-487">實作為應將非使用中的 FAT 和配置點陣圖視為過時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-487">Implementations shall consider the inactive FAT and Allocation Bitmap as stale.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-488">只有 TexFAT 感知的執行應該切換使用中的 FAT 和配置點陣圖 (請參閱 [7.1) 一節](#71-allocation-bitmap-directory-entry) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-488">Only TexFAT-aware implementations shall switch the active FAT and Allocation Bitmaps (see [Section 7.1](#71-allocation-bitmap-directory-entry)).</span></span>

##### <a name="31132-volumedirty-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-489">3.1.13.2 VolumeDirty 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-489">3.1.13.2 VolumeDirty Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-490">VolumeDirty 欄位應描述磁片區是否已變更，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-490">The VolumeDirty field shall describe whether the volume is dirty or not, as follows:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-491">0，表示磁片區可能處於一致的狀態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-491">0, which means the volume is probably in a consistent state</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-492">1，表示磁片區可能處於不一致的狀態</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-492">1, which means the volume is probably in an inconsistent state</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-493">在遇到無法解析的檔案系統中繼資料不一致時，實值應該將此欄位的值設定為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-493">Implementations should set the value of this field to 1 upon encountering file system metadata inconsistencies which they do not resolve.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-494">如果在裝載磁片區時，此欄位的值為1，則只有解析檔案系統中繼資料不一致的執行程式可能會將此欄位的值清除為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-494">If, upon mounting a volume, the value of this field is 1, only implementations which resolve file system metadata inconsistencies may clear the value of this field to 0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-495">這類的執行應該只在確定檔案系統處於一致狀態之後，才將此欄位的值清除為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-495">Such implementations shall only clear the value of this field to 0 after ensuring the file system is in a consistent state.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-496">如果在裝載磁片區時，此欄位的值為0，則在更新檔案系統中繼資料之前，應該將此欄位設定為1，並在之後將此欄位清除為0，類似于 [8.1 章節](#81-recommended-write-ordering)中所述的建議寫入順序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-496">If, upon mounting a volume, the value of this field is 0, implementations should set this field to 1 before updating file system metadata and clear this field to 0 afterwards, similar to the recommended write ordering described in [Section 8.1](#81-recommended-write-ordering).</span></span>

##### <a name="31133-mediafailure-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-497">3.1.13.3 MediaFailure 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-497">3.1.13.3 MediaFailure Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-498">MediaFailure 欄位應描述某個執行是否發現媒體失敗，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-498">The MediaFailure field shall describe whether an implementation has discovered media failures or not, as follows:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-499">0，表示裝載媒體尚未回報失敗，或任何已知的失敗都已記錄在 FAT 中為「不當」叢集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-499">0, which means the hosting media has not reported failures or any known failures are already recorded in the FAT as "bad" clusters</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-500">1，這表示裝載媒體已回報失敗 (亦即，讀取或寫入作業失敗) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-500">1, which means the hosting media has reported failures (i.e. has failed read or write operations)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-501">執行時，應該將此欄位設為1：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-501">An implementation should set this field to 1 when:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-502">裝載媒體無法嘗試存取磁片區中的任何區域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-502">The hosting media fails access attempts to any region in the volume</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-503">此執行已用盡存取重試演算法（如果有的話）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-503">The implementation has exhausted access retry algorithms, if any</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-504">如果在裝載磁片區時，此欄位的值為1，則為掃描整個磁片區以進行媒體故障的執行，並將所有失敗記錄為 FAT (的「不良」叢集，或以其他方式解決媒體失敗) 可能會將此欄位的值清除為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-504">If, upon mounting a volume, the value of this field is 1, implementations which scan the entire volume for media failures and record all failures as "bad" clusters in the FAT (or otherwise resolve media failures) may clear the value of this field to 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="31134-cleartozero-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-505">3.1.13.4 ClearToZero 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-505">3.1.13.4 ClearToZero Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-506">ClearToZero 欄位在此規格中沒有重大意義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-506">The ClearToZero field does not have significant meaning in this specification.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-507">此欄位的有效值為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-507">The valid values for this field are:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-508">0，沒有任何特殊意義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-508">0, which does not have any particular meaning</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-509">1，這表示在修改任何檔案系統結構、目錄或檔案之前，必須先將此欄位清除為0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-509">1, which means implementations shall clear this field to 0 prior to modifying any file system structures, directories, or files</span></span>

#### <a name="3114-bytespersectorshift-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-510">3.1.14 BytesPerSectorShift 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-510">3.1.14 BytesPerSectorShift Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-511">BytesPerSectorShift 欄位應描述每個磁區的位元組（以記錄<sub>2</sub> 表示） (N) ，其中 N 是每個磁區的位元組數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-511">The BytesPerSectorShift field shall describe the bytes per sector expressed as log<sub>2</sub>(N), where N is the number of bytes per sector.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-512">例如，針對每個磁區512個位元組，此欄位的值為9。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-512">For example, for 512 bytes per sector, the value of this field is 9.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-513">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-513">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-514">至少有9個 (磁區大小為512個位元組) ，這是 exFAT 磁片區的最小磁區</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-514">At least 9 (sector size of 512 bytes), which is the smallest sector possible for an exFAT volume</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-515">最多12個 (磁區大小為4096個位元組) ，也就是個人電腦中常見 Cpu 的記憶體頁面大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-515">At most 12 (sector size of 4096 bytes), which is the memory page size of CPUs common in personal computers</span></span>

#### <a name="3115-sectorsperclustershift-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-516">3.1.15 SectorsPerClusterShift 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-516">3.1.15 SectorsPerClusterShift Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-517">SectorsPerClusterShift 欄位應描述每個叢集的磁區（以記錄<sub>2</sub> (N) 表示），其中 n 是每個叢集的磁區數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-517">The SectorsPerClusterShift field shall describe the sectors per cluster expressed as log<sub>2</sub>(N), where N is number of sectors per cluster.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-518">例如，針對每個叢集8個磁區，此欄位的值為3。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-518">For example, for 8 sectors per cluster, the value of this field is 3.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-519">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-519">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-520">每個叢集至少有 0 (1 個磁區) ，也就是最小的叢集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-520">At least 0 (1 sector per cluster), which is the smallest cluster possible</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-521">最多25個 BytesPerSectorShift，其評估為 32 MB 的叢集大小</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-521">At most 25 - BytesPerSectorShift, which evaluates to a cluster size of 32MB</span></span>

#### <a name="3116-numberoffats-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-522">3.1.16 NumberOfFats 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-522">3.1.16 NumberOfFats Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-523">NumberOfFats 欄位應描述磁片區包含的 FATs 和配置點陣圖數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-523">The NumberOfFats field shall describe the number of FATs and Allocation Bitmaps the volume contains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-524">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-524">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-525">1，表示磁片區只包含第一個 FAT 和第一個配置點陣圖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-525">1, which indicates the volume only contains the First FAT and First Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-526">2，表示磁片區包含第一個 FAT、第二個 FAT、第一個配置點陣圖和第二個配置點陣圖;此值只對 TexFAT 磁片區有效</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-526">2, which indicates the volume contains the First FAT, Second FAT, First Allocation Bitmap, and Second Allocation Bitmap; this value is only valid for TexFAT volumes</span></span>

#### <a name="3117-driveselect-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-527">3.1.17 DriveSelect 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-527">3.1.17 DriveSelect Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-528">DriveSelect 欄位必須包含擴充的 INT 13h 磁片磁碟機編號，以協助在個人電腦上使用擴充的 INT 13h，從這個磁片區進行開機搭接接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-528">The DriveSelect field shall contain the extended INT 13h drive number, which aids boot-strapping from this volume using extended INT 13h on personal computers.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-529">此欄位的所有可能值都是有效的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-529">All possible values for this field are valid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-530">舊版 FAT 檔案系統中類似的欄位經常包含值80h。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-530">Similar fields in previous FAT-based file systems frequently contained the value 80h.</span></span>

#### <a name="3118-percentinuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-531">3.1.18 PercentInUse 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-531">3.1.18 PercentInUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-532">PercentInUse 欄位應描述叢集堆積中配置的群集百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-532">The PercentInUse field shall describe the percentage of clusters in the Cluster Heap which are allocated.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-533">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-533">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-534">介於0與100（含）之間，這是叢集堆積中已配置叢集的百分比，舍入到最接近的整數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-534">Between 0 and 100 inclusively, which is the percentage of allocated clusters in the Cluster Heap, rounded down to the nearest integer</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-535">完全 FFh，表示叢集堆積中配置的叢集百分比無法使用</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-535">Exactly FFh, which indicates the percentage of allocated clusters in the Cluster Heap is not available</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-536">「執行」應變更此欄位的值，以反映在叢集堆積中配置叢集的變更，或應該將它變更為 FFh。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-536">Implementations shall change the value of this field to reflect changes in the allocation of clusters in the Cluster Heap or shall change it to FFh.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-537">在計算其各自的主要開機或備份開機區域總和檢查碼時，不應包含此欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-537">Implementations shall not include this field when computing its respective Main Boot or Backup Boot region checksum.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-538">參考備份開機磁區時，執行應該會將此欄位視為過時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-538">When referring to the Backup Boot Sector, implementations shall treat this field as stale.</span></span>

#### <a name="3119-bootcode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-539">3.1.19 啟動代碼欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-539">3.1.19 BootCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-540">啟動控制欄位必須包含開機搭接接指令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-540">The BootCode field shall contain boot-strapping instructions.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-541">執行程式可能會在此欄位中填入開機-搭接接電腦系統所需的 CPU 指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-541">Implementations may populate this field with the CPU instructions necessary for boot-strapping a computer system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-542">未提供開機搭接接指令的執行程式應初始化此欄位中的每個位元組，以 F4h (個人電腦中常見 Cpu 的停止指令，) 作為其格式作業的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-542">Implementations which don't provide boot-strapping instructions shall initialize each byte in this field to F4h (the halt instruction for CPUs common in personal computers) as part of their format operation.</span></span>

#### <a name="3120-bootsignature-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-543">3.1.20 BootSignature 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-543">3.1.20 BootSignature Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-544">BootSignature 欄位應描述指定的磁區意圖是否為開機磁區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-544">The BootSignature field shall describe whether the intent of a given sector is for it to be a Boot Sector or not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-545">此欄位的有效值為 AA55h。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-545">The valid value for this field is AA55h.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-546">此欄位中的任何其他值都會使其各自的開機磁區失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-546">Any other value in this field invalidates its respective Boot Sector.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-547">根據其各自的開機磁區中的任何其他欄位，執行前應先驗證此欄位的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-547">Implementations should verify the contents of this field prior to depending on any other field in its respective Boot Sector.</span></span>

### <a name="32-main-and-backup-extended-boot-sectors-sub-regions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-548">3.2 主要和備份延伸開機磁區子領域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-548">3.2 Main and Backup Extended Boot Sectors Sub-regions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-549">主要延伸開機磁區的每個磁區都有相同的結構;不過，每個磁區都可能保存不同的開機搭接接指令 (請參閱表 6) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-549">Each sector of the Main Extended Boot Sectors has the same structure; however, each sector may hold distinct boot-strapping instructions (see Table 6).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-550">搭接接代理程式（例如主要開機磁區的開機搭接接指令、替代的 BIOS 程式或內嵌系統的固件）可能會載入這些磁區，並執行它們所包含的指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-550">Boot-strapping agents, such as the boot-strapping instructions in the Main Boot Sector, alternate BIOS implementations, or an embedded system's firmware, may load these sectors and execute the instructions they contain.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-551">備份擴充的開機磁區是主要延伸開機磁區的備份，而且具有相同的結構 (請參閱 [表 6](#table-6-extended-boot-sector-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-551">The Backup Extended Boot Sectors is a backup of the Main Extended Boot Sectors and has the same structure (see [Table 6](#table-6-extended-boot-sector-structure)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-552">在執行主要或備份擴充開機磁區的指示之前，執行程式應確定每個磁區的 ExtendedBootSignature 欄位都包含其指定的值，以驗證其內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-552">Prior to executing the instructions of either the Main or Backup Extended Boot Sectors, implementations should verify their contents by ensuring each sector's ExtendedBootSignature field contains its prescribed value.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-553">雖然初始格式作業將會初始化主要和備份延伸開機磁區的內容，但執行可能會將這些磁區 (更新，並且也應該視需要更新其各自的開機總和檢查碼) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-553">While the initial format operation will initialize the contents of both the Main and Backup Extended Boot Sectors, implementations may update these sectors (and shall also update their respective Boot Checksum) as needed.</span></span>

<p><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-570">注意：主要和備份開機磁區都包含 BytesPerSectorShift 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-570">Note: the Main and Backup Boot Sectors both contain the BytesPerSectorShift field.</span></span></p></td>

#### <a name="321-extendedbootcode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-571">3.2.1 ExtendedBootCode 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-571">3.2.1 ExtendedBootCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-572">ExtendedBootCode 欄位應包含開機搭接接指令。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-572">The ExtendedBootCode field shall contain boot-strapping instructions.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-573">執行程式可能會在此欄位中填入開機-搭接接電腦系統所需的 CPU 指示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-573">Implementations may populate this field with the CPU instructions necessary for boot-strapping a computer system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-574">未提供開機搭接接指示的執行，應該將此欄位中的每個位元組初始化為其格式作業的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-574">Implementations which don't provide boot-strapping instructions shall initialize each byte in this field to 00h as part of their format operation.</span></span>

#### <a name="322-extendedbootsignature-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-575">3.2.2 ExtendedBootSignature 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-575">3.2.2 ExtendedBootSignature Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-576">ExtendedBootSignature 欄位應描述指定的磁區意圖是否為擴充的開機磁區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-576">The ExtendedBootSignature field shall describe whether the intent of given sector is for it to be an Extended Boot Sector or not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-577">此欄位的有效值為 AA550000h。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-577">The valid value for this field is AA550000h.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-578">此欄位中的任何其他值都會使其各自的主要或備份擴充開機磁區失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-578">Any other value in this field invalidates its respective Main or Backup Extended Boot Sector.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-579">根據個別的擴充開機磁區中的任何其他欄位，執行前應該先驗證此欄位的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-579">Implementations should verify the contents of this field prior to depending on any other field in its respective Extended Boot Sector.</span></span>

### <a name="33-main-and-backup-oem-parameters-sub-regions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-580">3.3 主要和備份 OEM 參數子領域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-580">3.3 Main and Backup OEM Parameters Sub-regions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-581">主要 OEM 參數子領域包含十個參數結構，其中可能包含製造商專屬的資訊 (請參閱 [ [表 7](#table-7-oem-parameters-structure) ]) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-581">The Main OEM Parameters sub-region contains ten parameters structures which may contain manufacturer-specific information (see [Table 7](#table-7-oem-parameters-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-582">這十個參數結構中的每一個都是衍生自泛型參數範本 (請參閱 [3.3.2) 一節](#332-generic-parameters-template) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-582">Each of the ten parameters structures derives from the Generic Parameters template (see [Section 3.3.2](#332-generic-parameters-template)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-583">製造商可以從一般參數範本衍生自己的自訂參數結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-583">Manufacturers may derive their own custom parameters structures from the Generic Parameters template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-584">此規格本身會定義兩個參數結構： Null 參數 (請參閱 3.3.3) 和 Flash 參數 [一節](#333-null-parameters) (請參閱 [3.3.4) 一節](#334-flash-parameters) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-584">This specification itself defines two parameters structures: Null Parameters (see [Section 3.3.3](#333-null-parameters)) and Flash Parameters (see [Section 3.3.4](#334-flash-parameters)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-585">備份 OEM 參數是主要 OEM 參數的備份，且具有相同的結構 (請參閱 [ [表 7](#table-7-oem-parameters-structure) ]) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-585">The Backup OEM Parameters is a backup of the Main OEM Parameters and has the same structure (see [Table 7](#table-7-oem-parameters-structure)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-586">在使用主要或備份 OEM 參數的內容之前，必須先驗證其各自的開機總和檢查碼，以驗證其內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-586">Prior to using the contents of either the Main or Backup OEM Parameters, implementations shall verify their contents by validating their respective Boot Checksum.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-587">製造商應該使用自己的自訂參數結構（如果有的話）和任何其他參數結構來填入主要和備份 OEM 參數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-587">Manufacturers should populate the Main and Backup OEM Parameters with their own custom parameters structures, if any, and any other parameter structures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-588">後續的格式作業應該會保留主要和備份 OEM 參數的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-588">Subsequent format operations shall preserve the contents of the Main and Backup OEM Parameters.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-589">視需要更新主要和備份 OEM 參數 (，也應更新其各自的開機總和檢查碼) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-589">Implementations may update the Main and Backup OEM Parameters as needed (and shall also update their respective Boot Checksum).</span></span>

#### <a name="331-parameters0--parameters9"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-622">3.3.1 參數 \[ 0 \] .。。參數 \[ 9\]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-622">3.3.1 Parameters\[0\] ... Parameters\[9\]</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-623">這個陣列中的每個參數欄位都包含一個參數結構，此結構衍生自泛型參數範本 (請參閱 [3.3.2) 一節](#332-generic-parameters-template) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-623">Each Parameters field in this array contains a parameters structure, which derives from the Generic Parameters template (see [Section 3.3.2](#332-generic-parameters-template)).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-624">任何未使用的參數欄位都必須描述為包含 Null 參數結構 (請參閱 [3.3.3) 一節](#333-null-parameters) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-624">Any unused Parameters field shall be described as containing a Null Parameters structure (see [Section 3.3.3](#333-null-parameters)).</span></span>

#### <a name="332-generic-parameters-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-625">3.3.2 一般參數範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-625">3.3.2 Generic Parameters Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-626">泛型參數範本會提供參數結構的基底定義 (請參閱 [表 8](#table-8-generic-parameters-template)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-626">The Generic Parameters template provides the base definition of a parameters structure (see [Table 8](#table-8-generic-parameters-template)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-627">所有的參數結構都會衍生自這個範本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-627">All parameters structures derive from this template.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-628">此泛型參數範本的支援是必要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-628">Support for this Generic Parameters template is mandatory.</span></span>

##### <a name="3321-parametersguid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-644">3.3.2.1 ParametersGuid 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-644">3.3.2.1 ParametersGuid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-645">ParametersGuid 欄位必須描述 GUID，以決定指定參數結構的其餘部分的配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-645">The ParametersGuid field shall describe a GUID, which determines the layout of the remainder of the given parameters structure.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-646">此欄位的所有可能值都是有效的;不過，製造商應該使用 GUID 產生工具（例如 GuidGen.exe），從這個範本衍生自訂參數結構時選取 GUID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-646">All possible values for this field are valid; however, manufacturers should use a GUID-generating tool, such as GuidGen.exe, to select a GUID when deriving custom parameters structures from this template.</span></span>

#### <a name="333-null-parameters"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-647">3.3.3 Null 參數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-647">3.3.3 Null Parameters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-648">Null 參數結構衍生自泛型參數範本 (請參閱 [3.3.2 一節](#332-generic-parameters-template)) ，而且應該描述未使用的參數欄位 (請參閱 [ [表 9](#table-9-null-parameters-structure) ]) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-648">The Null Parameters structure derives from the Generic Parameters template (see [Section 3.3.2](#332-generic-parameters-template)) and shall describe an unused Parameters field (see [Table 9](#table-9-null-parameters-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-649">建立或更新 OEM 參數結構時，實值會以 Null 參數結構填入未使用的參數欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-649">When creating or updating the OEM Parameters structure, implementations shall populate unused Parameters fields with the Null Parameters structure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-650">此外，在建立或更新 OEM 參數結構時，實值應該在陣列的結尾合併 Null 參數結構，藉此將所有其他參數結構保留在 OEM 參數結構的開頭。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-650">Also, when creating or updating the OEM Parameters structure, implementations should consolidate Null Parameters structures at the end of the array, thereby leaving all other Parameters structures at the beginning of the OEM Parameters structure.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-651">Null 參數結構的支援是必要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-651">Support for the Null Parameters structure is mandatory.</span></span>

##### <a name="3331-parametersguid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-667">3.3.3.1 ParametersGuid 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-667">3.3.3.1 ParametersGuid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-668">ParametersGuid 欄位必須符合泛型參數範本所提供的定義 (請參閱 3.3.2.1) [一節](#3321-parametersguid-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-668">The ParametersGuid field shall conform to the definition provided by the Generic Parameters template (see [Section 3.3.2.1](#3321-parametersguid-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-669">此欄位的有效值（以 GUID 標記法表示）為 {00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000} 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-669">The valid value for this field, in GUID notation, is {00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000}.</span></span>

#### <a name="334-flash-parameters"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-670">3.3.4 Flash 參數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-670">3.3.4 Flash Parameters</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-671">Flash 參數結構衍生自「一般參數」範本 (請參閱 [3.3.2) 一節](#332-generic-parameters-template) ，其中包含 Flash 媒體的參數 (請參閱 [ [表 10](#table-10-flash-parameters-structure) ]) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-671">The Flash Parameter structure derives from the Generic Parameters template (see [Section 3.3.2](#332-generic-parameters-template)) and contains parameters for flash media (see [Table 10](#table-10-flash-parameters-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-672">Flash 型存放裝置的製造商可能會填入參數欄位， (最好是參數 \[ 0 \] 欄位) 使用此參數結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-672">Manufacturers of flash-based storage devices may populate a Parameters field (preferably the Parameters\[0\] field) with this parameters structure.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-673">執行程式可能會使用 Flash 參數結構中的資訊，將讀取/寫入期間的存取作業優化，以及調整媒體 durning 格式的檔案系統結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-673">Implementations may use the information in the Flash Parameters structure to optimize access operations during reads/writes and for alignment of file system structures durning formatting of the media.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-674">Flash 參數結構的支援是選擇性的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-674">Support for the Flash Parameters structure is optional.</span></span>

</table>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-718">所有 Flash 參數欄位的所有可能值（ParametersGuid 欄位除外）都是有效的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-718">All possible values for all Flash Parameters fields, except for the ParametersGuid field, are valid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-719">不過，值0表示欄位實際上是無意義的 (實作為應忽略指定的欄位) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-719">However, the value 0 indicates the field is actually meaningless (implementations shall ignore the given field).</span></span>

##### <a name="3341-parametersguid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-720">3.3.4.1 ParametersGuid 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-720">3.3.4.1 ParametersGuid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-721">ParametersGuid 欄位必須符合泛型參數範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 3.3.2.1) [一節](#3321-parametersguid-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-721">The ParametersGuid field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Parameters template (see [Section 3.3.2.1](#3321-parametersguid-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-722">此欄位的有效值（以 GUID 標記法表示）為 {0A0C7E46-3399-4021-90C8-FA6D389C4BA2}。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-722">The valid value for this field, in GUID notation, is {0A0C7E46-3399-4021-90C8-FA6D389C4BA2}.</span></span>

##### <a name="3342-eraseblocksize-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-723">3.3.4.2 EraseBlockSize 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-723">3.3.4.2 EraseBlockSize Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-724">EraseBlockSize 欄位應描述 flash 媒體清除區塊的大小（以位元組為單位）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-724">The EraseBlockSize field shall describe the size, in bytes, of the flash media's erase block.</span></span>

##### <a name="3343-pagesize-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-725">3.3.4.3 PageSize 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-725">3.3.4.3 PageSize Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-726">PageSize 欄位應描述 flash 媒體頁面的大小（以位元組為單位）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-726">The PageSize field shall describe the size, in bytes of the flash media's page.</span></span>

##### <a name="3344-sparesectors-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-727">3.3.4.4 SpareSectors 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-727">3.3.4.4 SpareSectors Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-728">SpareSectors 欄位應描述 flash 媒體可供其內部備用作業使用的磁區數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-728">The SpareSectors field shall describe the number of sectors the flash media has available for its internal sparing operations.</span></span>

##### <a name="3345-randomaccesstime-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-729">3.3.4.5 RandomAccessTime 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-729">3.3.4.5 RandomAccessTime Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-730">RandomAccessTime 欄位應描述 flash 媒體的平均隨機存取時間（以納秒為單位）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-730">The RandomAccessTime field shall describe the flash media's average random access time, in nanoseconds.</span></span>

##### <a name="3346-programmingtime-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-731">3.3.4.6 ProgrammingTime 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-731">3.3.4.6 ProgrammingTime Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-732">ProgrammingTime 欄位應描述 flash 媒體的平均程式設計時間（以毫微秒為單位）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-732">The ProgrammingTime field shall describe the flash media's average programming time, in nanoseconds.</span></span>

##### <a name="3347-readcycle-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-733">3.3.4.7 ReadCycle 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-733">3.3.4.7 ReadCycle Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-734">ReadCycle 欄位應描述 flash 媒體的平均讀取週期時間（以毫微秒為單位）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-734">The ReadCycle field shall describe the flash media's average read cycle time, in nanoseconds.</span></span>

##### <a name="3348-writecycle-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-735">3.3.4.8 WriteCycle 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-735">3.3.4.8 WriteCycle Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-736">WriteCycle 欄位應該描述平均寫入週期時間（以納秒為單位）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-736">The WriteCycle field shall describe the average write cycle time, in nanoseconds.</span></span>

### <a name="34-main-and-backup-boot-checksum-sub-regions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-737">3.4 主要和備份開機總和檢查碼子領域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-737">3.4 Main and Backup Boot Checksum Sub-regions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-738">主要和備份開機總和檢查碼各自包含各自的開機區域中，所有其他子領域之內容的四位元組總和檢查碼的重複模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-738">The Main and Backup Boot Checksums each contain a repeating pattern of the four-byte checksum of the contents of all other sub-regions in their respective Boot regions.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-739">總和檢查碼計算不應該在其各自的開機磁區中包含 VolumeFlags 和 PercentInUse 欄位 (請參閱 [ [圖 1](#figure-1-boot-checksum-computation) ]) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-739">The checksum calculation shall not include the VolumeFlags and PercentInUse fields in their respective Boot Sector (see [Figure 1](#figure-1-boot-checksum-computation)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-740">四位元組總和檢查碼的重複模式會將其各自的開機總和檢查碼子領域從子領域的開頭填滿。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-740">The repeating pattern of the four-byte checksum fills its respective Boot Checksum sub-region from the beginning to the end of the sub-region.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-741">在主要或備份啟動區域中使用任何其他子領域的內容之前，必須先驗證其各自的開機總和檢查碼，以驗證它們的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-741">Prior to using the contents of any of the other sub-regions in either the Main or Backup Boot regions, implementations shall verify their contents by validating their respective Boot Checksum.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-742">初始格式作業會將主要和備份開機總和檢查碼填入重複的總和檢查碼模式，而在其個別開機區域中的其他磁區內容變更時，則必須更新這些磁區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-742">While the initial format operation will populate both the Main and Backup Boot Checksums with the repeating checksum pattern, implementations shall update these sectors as the contents of the other sectors in their respective Boot regions change.</span></span>

<div id="figure-1-boot-checksum-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-743">**圖1開機總和檢查碼計算**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-743">**Figure 1 Boot Checksum Computation**</span></span>

```c
UInt32 BootChecksum
(
    UCHAR  * Sectors,        // points to an in-memory copy of the 11 sectors
    USHORT   BytesPerSector
)
{
    UInt32 NumberOfBytes = (UInt32)BytesPerSector * 11;
    UInt32 Checksum = 0;
    UInt32 Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < NumberOfBytes; Index++)
    {
        if ((Index == 106) || (Index == 107) || (Index == 112))
        {
            continue;
        }
        Checksum = ((Checksum&1) ? 0x80000000 : 0) + (Checksum>>1) + (UInt32)Sectors[Index];
    }

    return Checksum;
}
```

## <a name="4-file-allocation-table-region"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-744">4個檔案配置資料表區域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-744">4 File Allocation Table Region</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-745">檔案配置表 (FAT) 區域最多可包含兩個 FATs，一個位於第一個 FAT 子領域，另一個位於第二個 FAT 子領域。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-745">The File Allocation Table (FAT) region may contain up to two FATs, one in the First FAT sub-region and another in the Second FAT sub-region.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-746">NumberOfFats 欄位描述此區域包含的 FATs 數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-746">The NumberOfFats field describes how many FATs this region contains.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-747">NumberOfFats 欄位的有效值為1和2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-747">The valid values for the NumberOfFats field are 1 and 2.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-748">因此，第一個 FAT 子領域一律會包含 FAT。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-748">Therefore, the First FAT sub-region always contains a FAT.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-749">如果 NumberOfFats 欄位是2，則第二個 FAT 子領域也會包含 FAT。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-749">If the NumberOfFats field is two, then the Second FAT sub-region also contains a FAT.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-750">[VolumeFlags] 欄位的 [ActiveFat] 欄位描述作用中的是哪個 FAT。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-750">The ActiveFat field of the VolumeFlags field describes which FAT is active.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-751">只有主要開機磁區中的 VolumeFlags 欄位是最新的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-751">Only the VolumeFlags field in the Main Boot Sector is current.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-752">必須將不是作用中的 FAT 視為過時。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-752">Implementations shall treat the FAT which is not active as stale.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-753">使用非使用中的 FAT 和在 FATs 之間切換是特定的執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-753">Use of the inactive FAT and switching between FATs is implementation specific.</span></span>

### <a name="41-first-and-second-fat-sub-regions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-754">4.1 第一個和第二個 FAT 子領域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-754">4.1 First and Second FAT Sub-regions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-755">FAT 應描述叢集堆積中的叢集鏈 (請參閱 [表 11](#table-11-file-allocation-table-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-755">A FAT shall describe cluster chains in the Cluster Heap (see [Table 11](#table-11-file-allocation-table-structure)).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-756">叢集鏈是一系列的群集，可提供空間來記錄檔案、目錄和其他檔案系統結構的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-756">A cluster chain is a series of clusters which provides space for recording the contents of files, directories, and other file system structures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-757">FAT 將叢集鏈表示為叢集索引的單一連結清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-757">A FAT represents a cluster chain as a singly-linked list of cluster indices.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-758">除了前兩個專案之外，每個 FAT 中的每個專案都只代表一個群集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-758">With the exception of the first two entries, every entry in a FAT represents exactly one cluster.</span></span>

#### <a name="411-fatentry0-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-801">4.1.1 FatEntry \[ 0 \] 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-801">4.1.1 FatEntry\[0\] Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-802">FatEntry \[ 0 \] 欄位應描述第一個位元組中的媒體類型 (最低順序位元組) ，而且在其餘三個位元組中應包含 FFh。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-802">The FatEntry\[0\] field shall describe the media type in the first byte (the lowest order byte) and shall contain FFh in the remaining three bytes.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-803">應 F8h 第一個位元組)  (的媒體類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-803">The media type (the first byte) should be F8h.</span></span>

#### <a name="412-fatentry1-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-804">4.1.2 FatEntry \[ 1 \] 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-804">4.1.2 FatEntry\[1\] Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-805">FatEntry \[ 1 \] 欄位只會因為歷程記錄優先順序而存在，而且不會描述感興趣的任何事物。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-805">The FatEntry\[1\] field only exists due to historical precedence and does not describe anything of interest.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-806">此欄位的有效值為 FFFFFFFFh。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-806">The valid value for this field is FFFFFFFFh.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-807">實值應該將此欄位初始化為其指定的值，而且不應該將此欄位用於任何用途。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-807">Implementations shall initialize this field to its prescribed value and should not use this field for any purpose.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-808">「執行」不應解讀此欄位，而且應該在修改周圍欄位的作業之間保留其內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-808">Implementations should not interpret this field and shall preserve its contents across operations which modify surrounding fields.</span></span>

#### <a name="413-fatentry2--fatentryclustercount1-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-809">4.1.3 FatEntry \[ 2 \] .。。FatEntry \[ ClusterCount + 1 個 \] 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-809">4.1.3 FatEntry\[2\] ... FatEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-810">此陣列中的每個 FatEntry 欄位都應代表叢集堆積中的叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-810">Each FatEntry field in this array shall represent a cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-811">FatEntry \[ 2 \] 代表叢集堆積中的第一個叢集，而 FatEntry \[ ClusterCount + 1 代表叢集中的 \] 最後一個叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-811">FatEntry\[2\] represents the first cluster in the Cluster Heap and FatEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] represents the last cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-812">這些欄位之值的有效範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-812">The valid range of values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-813">介於2和 ClusterCount + 1 之間（含），指向指定叢集鏈中的下一個 FatEntry;指定的 FatEntry 不應指向位於指定叢集鏈中的任何 FatEntry</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-813">Between 2 and ClusterCount + 1, inclusively, which points to the next FatEntry in the given cluster chain; the given FatEntry shall not point to any FatEntry which precedes it in the given cluster chain</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-814">完全 FFFFFFF7h，將指定 FatEntry 的對應叢集標示為「不良」</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-814">Exactly FFFFFFF7h, which marks the given FatEntry's corresponding cluster as "bad"</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-815">完全 FFFFFFFFh，它會將指定的 FatEntry 對應叢集標示為叢集鏈的最後一個叢集;這是任何指定叢集鏈最後一個 FatEntry 的唯一有效值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-815">Exactly FFFFFFFFh, which marks the given FatEntry's corresponding cluster as the last cluster of a cluster chain; this is the only valid value for the last FatEntry of any given cluster chain</span></span>

## <a name="5-data-region"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-816">5個數據區域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-816">5 Data Region</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-817">資料區域包含叢集堆積，可為檔案系統結構、目錄和檔案提供受控空間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-817">The Data region contains the Cluster Heap, which provides managed space for file system structures, directories, and files.</span></span>

### <a name="51-cluster-heap-sub-region"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-818">5.1 叢集堆積子領域</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-818">5.1 Cluster Heap Sub-region</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-819">叢集堆積的結構非常簡單 (請參閱 [表 12](#table-12-cluster-heap-structure)) ;每一系列連續的磁區都會描述一個叢集，如同 SectorsPerClusterShift 欄位所定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-819">The Cluster Heap's structure is very simple (see [Table 12](#table-12-cluster-heap-structure)); each consecutive series of sectors describes one cluster, as the SectorsPerClusterShift field defines.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-820">重要的是，叢集堆積的第一個叢集有索引二，這會直接對應至 FatEntry 2 的索引 \[ \] 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-820">Importantly, the first cluster of the Cluster Heap has index two, which directly corresponds to the index of FatEntry\[2\].</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-821">在 exFAT 磁片區中，配置點陣圖 (請參閱 [7.1.5 區段](#715-allocation-bitmap) ，) 維護所有叢集之配置狀態的記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-821">In an exFAT volume, an Allocation Bitmap (see [Section 7.1.5](#715-allocation-bitmap)) maintains the record of the allocation state of all clusters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-822">這與 exFAT 的前身 (FAT12、FAT16 和 FAT32) 有很大的差異，其中 FAT 會維護叢集堆積中所有叢集的配置狀態記錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-822">This is a significant difference from exFAT's predecessors (FAT12, FAT16, and FAT32), in which a FAT maintained a record of the allocation state of all clusters in the Cluster Heap.</span></span>

#### <a name="511-cluster2--clusterclustercount1-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-852">5.1.1 Cluster \[ 2 \] .。。Cluster \[ ClusterCount + 1 個 \] 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-852">5.1.1 Cluster\[2\] ... Cluster\[ClusterCount+1\] Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-853">此陣列中的每個叢集欄位都是一連串連續的磁區，其大小是由 SectorsPerClusterShift 欄位所定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-853">Each Cluster field in this array is a series of contiguous sectors, whose size is defined by the SectorsPerClusterShift field.</span></span>

## <a name="6-directory-structure"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-854">6個目錄結構</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-854">6 Directory Structure</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-855">ExFAT 檔案系統使用目錄樹狀結構方法來管理存在於叢集堆積中的檔案系統結構和檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-855">The exFAT file system uses a directory tree approach to manage the file system structures and files which exist in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-856">目錄樹狀結構中的父系和子系之間的目錄具有一對多關聯性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-856">Directories have a one-to-many relationship between parent and child in the directory tree.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-857">FirstClusterOfRootDirectory 欄位所參考的目錄是目錄樹狀結構的根。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-857">The directory to which the FirstClusterOfRootDirectory field refers is the root of the directory tree.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-858">所有其他目錄都會以單向連結的方式從根目錄中下降。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-858">All other directories descend from the root directory in a singly-linked fashion.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-859">每個目錄都是由一系列的目錄專案所組成 (請參閱 [ [表 13](#table-13-directory-structure) ]) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-859">Each directory consists of a series of directory entries (see [Table 13](#table-13-directory-structure)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-860">一或多個目錄專案會合並到目錄專案集，以描述感興趣的內容，例如檔案系統結構、子目錄或檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-860">One or more directory entries combine into a directory entry set which describes something of interest, such as a file system structure, sub-directory, or file.</span></span>
