### <a name="61-directoryentry0--directoryentryn--1"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-889">6.1 DirectoryEntry \[ 0 \] .。。DirectoryEntry \[ N--1\]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-889">6.1 DirectoryEntry\[0\] ... DirectoryEntry\[N--1\]</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-890">這個陣列中的每個 DirectoryEntry 欄位都是衍生自一般 DirectoryEntry 範本 (請參閱 [6.2) 一節](#62-generic-directoryentry-template) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-890">Each DirectoryEntry field in this array derives from the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2](#62-generic-directoryentry-template)).</span></span>

### <a name="62-generic-directoryentry-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-891">6.2 一般 DirectoryEntry 範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-891">6.2 Generic DirectoryEntry Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-892">一般 DirectoryEntry 範本會提供目錄專案的基底定義 (請參閱 [表 14](#table-14-generic-directoryentry-template)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-892">The Generic DirectoryEntry template provides the base definition for directory entries (see [Table 14](#table-14-generic-directoryentry-template)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-893">所有的目錄專案結構都是衍生自這個範本，而且只有 Microsoft 定義的目錄輸入結構有效 (exFAT 除了 [7.8 節](#78-vendor-extension-directory-entry) 和 [7.9 節](#79-vendor-allocation-directory-entry)) 中所定義以外，不會提供製造商定義之目錄輸入結構的規定。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-893">All directory entry structures derive from this template and only Microsoft-defined directory entry structures are valid (exFAT does not have provisions for manufacturer-defined directory entry structures except as defined in [Section 7.8](#78-vendor-extension-directory-entry) and [Section 7.9](#79-vendor-allocation-directory-entry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-894">可解讀泛型 DirectoryEntry 範本的功能是必要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-894">The ability to interpret the Generic DirectoryEntry template is mandatory.</span></span>

#### <a name="621-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-918">6.2.1 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-918">6.2.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-919">>entrytype 欄位有三種使用模式，欄位的值會定義 (請參閱以下) 的清單。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-919">The EntryType field has three modes of usage which the value of the field defines (see list below).</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-920">00h （這是目錄結束記號，並適用下列條件）：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-920">00h, which is an end-of-directory marker and the following conditions apply:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-921">指定 DirectoryEntry 中的所有其他欄位實際上都是保留的</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-921">All other fields in the given DirectoryEntry are actually reserved</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-922">指定目錄中的所有後續目錄專案也都是目錄結束記號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-922">All subsequent directory entries in the given directory also are end-of-directory markers</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-923">目錄結束記號只在目錄專案集外有效</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-923">End-of-directory markers are only valid outside directory entry sets</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-924">視需要覆寫可能會覆寫目錄結尾的標記</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-924">Implementations may overwrite end-of-directory markers as necessary</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-925">介於01h 和7Fh （可為）之間，這是未使用的目錄專案標記，而且適用下列情況：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-925">Between 01h and 7Fh inclusively, which is an unused-directory-entry marker and the following conditions apply:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-926">指定 DirectoryEntry 中的所有其他欄位實際上都未定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-926">All other fields in the given DirectoryEntry are actually undefined</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-927">未使用的目錄專案只在目錄專案集之外有效</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-927">Unused directory entries are only valid outside of directory entry sets</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-928">視需要覆寫可能會覆寫未使用的目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-928">Implementations may overwrite unused directory entries as necessary</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-929">這一範圍的值會對應到 InUse 欄位 (請參閱 [區段 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)) ，其中包含值0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-929">This range of values corresponds to the InUse field (see [Section 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)) containing the value 0</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-930">在81h 與 FFh 之間，其為一般目錄專案，而且適用下列條件：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-930">Between 81h and FFh inclusively, which is a regular directory entry and the following conditions apply:</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-931">>entrytype 欄位的內容 (請參閱 [表 15](#table-15-generic-entrytype-field-structure)) 判斷 DirectoryEntry 結構其餘部分的版面配置</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-931">The contents of the EntryType field (see [Table 15](#table-15-generic-entrytype-field-structure)) determine the layout of the remainder of the DirectoryEntry structure</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-932">此值範圍（只有此值範圍）在目錄專案集內是有效的</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-932">This range of values, and only this range of values, are valid inside a directory entry set</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-933">這一範圍的值會直接對應到 InUse 欄位 (請參閱) 包含值1的[區段 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-933">This range of values directly corresponds to the InUse field (see [Section 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)) containing the value 1</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-934">若要防止修改 InUse 欄位 (請參閱) [6.2.1.4 一節](#6214-inuse-field) ，以錯誤的方式產生目錄結束記號，值80h 無效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-934">To prevent modifications to the InUse field (see [Section 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)) erroneously resulting in an end-of-directory marker, the value 80h is invalid.</span></span>

##### <a name="6211-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-958">6.2.1.1 TypeCode 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-958">6.2.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-959">TypeCode 欄位會部分描述指定之目錄專案的特定類型。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-959">The TypeCode field partially describes the specific type of the given directory entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-960">此欄位加上 TypeImportance 和 TypeCategory 欄位 (分別參閱6.2.1.2 和[section 6.2.1.3](#6213-typecategory-field)[一節](#6212-typeimportance-field)，) 唯一識別指定目錄專案的型別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-960">This field, plus the TypeImportance and TypeCategory fields (see [Section 6.2.1.2](#6212-typeimportance-field) and [Section 6.2.1.3](#6213-typecategory-field), respectively) uniquely identify the type of the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-961">除非 TypeImportance 和 TypeCategory 欄位都包含0值，否則此欄位的所有可能值都是有效的。在此情況下，值0對此欄位而言是不正確。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-961">All possible values of this field are valid, unless the TypeImportance and TypeCategory fields both contain the value 0; in that case, the value 0 is invalid for this field.</span></span>

##### <a name="6212-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-962">6.2.1.2 TypeImportance 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-962">6.2.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-963">TypeImportance 欄位必須描述指定之目錄專案的重要性。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-963">The TypeImportance field shall describe the importance of the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-964">此欄位的有效值應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-964">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-965">0表示指定的目錄專案很重要 (請分別參閱重要主要和重要次要目錄專案的6.3.1.2.1 和[區段 6.4.1.2.1](#64121-critical-secondary-directory-entries) [一](#63121-critical-primary-directory-entries)節) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-965">0, which means the given directory entry is critical (see [Section    6.3.1.2.1](#63121-critical-primary-directory-entries) and [Section 6.4.1.2.1](#64121-critical-secondary-directory-entries) for critical primary and critical secondary   directory entries, respectively)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-966">1，這表示指定的目錄專案是良性的 (參閱 [6.3.1.2.2](#63122-benign-primary-directory-entries) 和 [6.4.1.2.2](#64122-benign-secondary-directory-entries) 一節，以取得無害的主要和良性次要目錄專案，分別是) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-966">1, which means the given directory entry is benign (see [Section    6.3.1.2.2](#63122-benign-primary-directory-entries) and [Section 6.4.1.2.2](#64122-benign-secondary-directory-entries) for benign primary and benign secondary   directory entries, respectively)</span></span>

##### <a name="6213-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-967">6.2.1.3 TypeCategory 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-967">6.2.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-968">TypeCategory 欄位必須描述指定之目錄專案的類別。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-968">The TypeCategory field shall describe the category of the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-969">此欄位的有效值應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-969">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-970">0，表示指定的目錄專案是主要 (請參閱 [6.3 節](#63-generic-primary-directoryentry-template)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-970">0, which means the given directory entry is primary (see [Section 6.3](#63-generic-primary-directoryentry-template))</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-971">1，表示指定的目錄專案是次要 (請參閱 [6.4 節](#64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-971">1, which means the given directory entry is secondary (see [Section 6.4](#64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template))</span></span>

##### <a name="6214-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-972">6.2.1.4 InUse 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-972">6.2.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-973">InUse 欄位應描述是否正在使用指定的目錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-973">The InUse field shall describe whether the given directory entry in use or not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-974">此欄位的有效值應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-974">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-975">0，表示指定的目錄專案未使用;這表示指定的結構實際上是未使用的目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-975">0, which means the given directory entry is not in use; this means the given structure actually is an unused directory entry</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-976">1，表示指定的目錄專案正在使用中;這表示指定的結構是一般目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-976">1, which means the given directory entry is in use; this means the given structure is a regular directory entry</span></span>

#### <a name="622-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-977">6.2.2 FirstCluster 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-977">6.2.2 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-978">FirstCluster 欄位必須包含與給定目錄專案相關聯之叢集堆積中配置的第一個叢集索引。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-978">The FirstCluster field shall contain the index of the first cluster of an allocation in the Cluster Heap associated with the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-979">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-979">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-980">正好是0，表示沒有叢集配置存在</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-980">Exactly 0, which means no cluster allocation exists</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-981">介於2和 ClusterCount + 1 之間，也就是有效叢集索引的範圍</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-981">Between 2 and ClusterCount + 1, which is the range of valid cluster indices</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-982">如果叢集配置與衍生結構不相容，則衍生自這個範本的結構可能會重新定義 FirstCluster 和 DataLength 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-982">Structures which derive from this template may redefine both the FirstCluster and DataLength fields, if a cluster allocation is not compatible with the derivative structure.</span></span>

#### <a name="623-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-983">上面 6.2.3 DataLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-983">6.2.3 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-984">DataLength 欄位描述相關聯的叢集配置所包含之資料的大小（以位元組為單位）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-984">The DataLength field describes the size, in bytes, of the data the associated cluster allocation contains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-985">此欄位值的有效範圍為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-985">The valid range of value for this field is:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-986">至少為 0;如果 FirstCluster 欄位包含值0，則這個欄位的唯一有效值為0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-986">At least 0; if the FirstCluster field contains the value 0, then this field's only valid value is 0</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-987">最多 ClusterCount \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup> \* 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup></span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-987">At most ClusterCount \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>\* 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup></span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-988">如果衍生結構無法進行叢集配置，則從這個範本衍生的結構可能會重新定義 FirstCluster 和 DataLength 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-988">Structures which derive from this template may redefine both the FirstCluster and DataLength fields, if a cluster allocation is not possible for the derivative structure.</span></span>

### <a name="63-generic-primary-directoryentry-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-989">6.3 一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-989">6.3 Generic Primary DirectoryEntry Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-990">目錄專案集的第一個目錄專案必須是主要目錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-990">The first directory entry in a directory entry set shall be a primary directory entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-991">目錄專案組中所有後續的目錄專案（如果有的話）都必須是次要目錄專案 (請參閱 [6.4) 一節](#64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-991">All subsequent directory entries, if any, in the directory entry set shall be secondary directory entries (see [Section 6.4](#64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-992">可解讀泛型主要 DirectoryEntry 範本的功能是必要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-992">The ability to interpret the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template is mandatory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-993">所有的主要目錄專案結構都衍生自一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本 (請參閱) 衍生自一般 DirectoryEntry 範本的 [ [表 16](#table-16-generic-primary-directoryentry-template) ]， (參閱 [6.2) 一節](#62-generic-directoryentry-template) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-993">All primary directory entry structures derive from the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Table 16](#table-16-generic-primary-directoryentry-template)), which derives from the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2](#62-generic-directoryentry-template)).</span></span>

#### <a name="631-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1029">6.3.1 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1029">6.3.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1030">>entrytype 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1) [一節](#621-entrytype-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1030">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1](#621-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="6311-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1031">6.3.1.1 TypeCode 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1031">6.3.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1032">TypeCode 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1.1) [一節](#6211-typecode-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1032">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.1](#6211-typecode-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="6312-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1033">6.3.1.2 TypeImportance 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1033">6.3.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1034">TypeImportance 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1.2) [一節](#6212-typeimportance-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1034">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.2](#6212-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

###### <a name="63121-critical-primary-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1035">6.3.1.2.1 重要的主要目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1035">6.3.1.2.1 Critical Primary Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1036">重要的主要目錄專案包含對 exFAT 磁片區適當管理很重要的資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1036">Critical primary directory entries contain information which is critical to the proper management of an exFAT volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1037">只有根目錄包含重要的主要目錄專案 (檔案目錄專案是例外狀況，請參閱 [7.4 節](#74-file-directory-entry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1037">Only the root directory contains critical primary directory entries (File directory entries are an exception, see [Section 7.4](#74-file-directory-entry)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1038">重要主要目錄專案的定義與主要 exFAT 修訂編號相關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1038">The definition of critical primary directory entries correlates to the major exFAT revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1039">執行必須支援所有重要的主要目錄專案，而且只會記錄此規格所定義的重要主要目錄專案結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1039">Implementations shall support all critical primary directory entries and shall only record the critical primary directory entry structures this specification defines.</span></span>

###### <a name="63122-benign-primary-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1040">6.3.1.2.2 良性的主要目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1040">6.3.1.2.2 Benign Primary Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1041">無害的主要目錄專案包含額外的資訊，可能有助於管理 exFAT 磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1041">Benign primary directory entries contain additional information which may be useful for managing an exFAT volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1042">任何目錄都可能包含良性的主要目錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1042">Any directory may contain benign primary directory entries.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1043">良性主要目錄專案的定義與次要 exFAT 修訂編號相關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1043">The definition of benign primary directory entries correlates to the minor exFAT revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1044">此規格或任何後續規格的任何良性主要目錄專案支援都是選擇性的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1044">Support for any benign primary directory entry this specification, or any subsequent specification, defines is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1045">無法辨識的良性主要目錄專案會將整個目錄專案集轉譯為無法辨識的 (，超出適用的目錄專案範本) 的定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1045">An unrecognized benign primary directory entry renders the entire directory entry set as unrecognized (beyond the definition of the applicable directory entry templates).</span></span>

##### <a name="6313-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1046">6.3.1.3 TypeCategory 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1046">6.3.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1047">TypeCategory 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1.3) [一節](#6213-typecategory-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1047">The TypeCategory field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.3](#6213-typecategory-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1048">針對此範本，此欄位的有效值應為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1048">For this template, the valid value for this field shall be 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="6314-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1049">6.3.1.4 InUse 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1049">6.3.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1050">InUse 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1.4) [一節](#6214-inuse-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1050">The InUse field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="632-secondarycount-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1051">6.3.2 SecondaryCount 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1051">6.3.2 SecondaryCount Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1052">SecondaryCount 欄位應描述緊接在指定的主要目錄專案後面的次要目錄專案數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1052">The SecondaryCount field shall describe the number of secondary directory entries which immediately follow the given primary directory entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1053">這些次要目錄專案以及指定的主要目錄專案，包含目錄專案集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1053">These secondary directory entries, along with the given primary directory entry, comprise the directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1054">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1054">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1055">至少為0，表示此主要目錄專案是目錄專案集中唯一的專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1055">At least 0, which means this primary directory entry is the only entry in the directory entry set</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1056">最多255，這表示下一個255目錄專案和此主要目錄專案組成目錄專案集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1056">At most 255, which means the next 255 directory entries and this primary directory entry comprise the directory entry set</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1057">從這個範本衍生的重要主要目錄專案結構可能會重新定義 SecondaryCount 和 SetChecksum 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1057">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine both the SecondaryCount and SetChecksum fields.</span></span>

#### <a name="633-setchecksum-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1058">6.3.3 SetChecksum 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1058">6.3.3 SetChecksum Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1059">SetChecksum 欄位應包含指定目錄專案集中所有目錄專案的總和檢查碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1059">The SetChecksum field shall contain the checksum of all directory entries in the given directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1060">不過，總和檢查碼會排除此欄位 (請參閱 [ [圖 2](#figure-2-entrysetchecksum-computation) ]) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1060">However, the checksum excludes this field (see [Figure 2](#figure-2-entrysetchecksum-computation)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1061">在使用指定的目錄專案集內的任何其他目錄專案之前，必須先驗證此欄位的內容是否有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1061">Implementations shall verify the contents of this field are valid prior to using any other directory entry in the given directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1062">從這個範本衍生的重要主要目錄專案結構可能會重新定義 SecondaryCount 和 SetChecksum 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1062">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine both the SecondaryCount and SetChecksum fields.</span></span>

<div id="figure-2-entrysetchecksum-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1063">**圖 2 EntrySetChecksum 計算**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1063">**Figure 2 EntrySetChecksum Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt16 EntrySetChecksum
(
    UCHAR * Entries,       // points to an in-memory copy of the directory entry set
    UCHAR   SecondaryCount
)
{
    UInt16 NumberOfBytes = ((UInt16)SecondaryCount + 1) * 32;
    UInt16 Checksum = 0;
    UInt16 Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < NumberOfBytes; Index++)
    {
        if ((Index == 2) || (Index == 3))
        {
            continue;
        }
        Checksum = ((Checksum&1) ? 0x8000 : 0) + (Checksum>>1) +  (UInt16)Entries[Index];
    }
    return Checksum;
}
```

#### <a name="634-generalprimaryflags-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1064">6.3.4 GeneralPrimaryFlags 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1064">6.3.4 GeneralPrimaryFlags Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1065">GeneralPrimaryFlags 欄位包含旗標 (請參閱 [表 17](#table-17-generic-generalprimaryflags-field-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1065">The GeneralPrimaryFlags field contains flags (see [Table 17](#table-17-generic-generalprimaryflags-field-structure)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1066">從這個範本衍生的重要主要目錄專案結構可能會重新定義此欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1066">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine this field.</span></span>

##### <a name="6341-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1086">6.3.4.1 AllocationPossible 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1086">6.3.4.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1087">AllocationPossible 欄位說明是否可以針對指定的目錄專案，描述叢集堆積中的配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1087">The AllocationPossible field shall describe whether or not an allocation in the Cluster Heap is possible for the given directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1088">此欄位的有效值應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1088">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1089">0表示無法建立相關聯的叢集配置，且 FirstCluster 和 DataLength 欄位實際上是未定義的 (結構（衍生自這個範本）可能會重新定義這些欄位) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1089">0, which means an associated allocation of clusters is not possible and the FirstCluster and DataLength fields are actually undefined (structures which derive from this template may redefine those fields)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1090">1，表示可以有相關聯的叢集配置，且 FirstCluster 和 DataLength 欄位已定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1090">1, which means an associated allocation of clusters is possible and the FirstCluster and DataLength fields are as defined</span></span>

##### <a name="6342-nofatchain-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1091">6.3.4.2 NoFatChain 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1091">6.3.4.2 NoFatChain Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1092">NoFatChain 欄位會指出作用中的 FAT 是否描述指定配置的叢集鏈。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1092">The NoFatChain field shall indicate whether or not the active FAT describes the given allocation's cluster chain.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1093">此欄位的有效值應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1093">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1094">0，這表示配置的叢集鏈的對應 FAT 專案是有效的，而且必須加以解讀。如果 AllocationPossible 欄位包含值0，或如果 AllocationPossible 欄位包含值1，且 FirstCluster 欄位包含值0，則這個欄位的唯一有效值為0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1094">0, which means the corresponding FAT entries for the allocation's cluster chain are valid and implementations shall interpret them; if the AllocationPossible field contains the value 0, or if the AllocationPossible field contains the value 1 and the FirstCluster field contains the value 0, then this field's only valid value is 0</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1095">1，這表示相關聯的配置是一系列連續的群集;叢集的對應 FAT 專案無效，且不應解讀它們;執行可能會使用下列方程式來計算關聯配置的大小： DataLength/ (2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup> \* 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>) 進位到最接近的整數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1095">1, which means the associated allocation is one contiguous series of clusters; the corresponding FAT entries for the clusters are invalid and implementations shall not interpret them; implementations may use the following equation to calculate the size of the associated allocation: DataLength / (2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>\* 2<sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>) rounded up to the nearest integer</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1096">如果從這個範本衍生的重要主要目錄專案結構重新定義 GeneralPrimaryFlags 欄位，則任何相關聯配置之叢集鏈的對應 FAT 專案都是有效的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1096">If critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template redefine the GeneralPrimaryFlags field, then the corresponding FAT entries for any associated allocation's cluster chain are valid.</span></span>

#### <a name="635-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1097">6.3.5 FirstCluster 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1097">6.3.5 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1098">FirstCluster 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.2) [一節](#622-firstcluster-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1098">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.2](#622-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1099">如果 NoFatChain 位為1，則 FirstCluster 必須指向叢集堆積中的有效群集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1099">If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then FirstCluster must point to a valid cluster in the cluster heap.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1100">從這個範本衍生的重要主要目錄專案結構可能會重新定義 FirstCluster 和 DataLength 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1100">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine the FirstCluster and DataLength fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1101">只有當 AllocationPossible 欄位包含值0時，其他衍生自這個範本的結構才可以重新定義 FirstCluster 和 DataLength 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1101">Other structures which derive from this template may redefine the FirstCluster and DataLength fields only if the AllocationPossible field contains the value 0.</span></span>

#### <a name="636-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1102">6.3.6 DataLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1102">6.3.6 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1103">DataLength 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱上面 6.2.3) [一節](#623-datalength-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1103">The DataLength field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.3](#623-datalength-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1104">如果 NoFatChain 位為1，則 DataLength 不得為零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1104">If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then DataLength must not be zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1105">如果 FirstCluster 欄位為零，則 DataLength 也必須為零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1105">If the FirstCluster field is zero, then DataLength must also be zero.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1106">從這個範本衍生的重要主要目錄專案結構可能會重新定義 FirstCluster 和 DataLength 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1106">Critical primary directory entry structures which derive from this template may redefine the FirstCluster and DataLength fields.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1107">只有當 AllocationPossible 欄位包含值0時，其他衍生自這個範本的結構才可以重新定義 FirstCluster 和 DataLength 欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1107">Other structures which derive from this template may redefine the FirstCluster and DataLength fields only if the AllocationPossible field contains the value 0.</span></span>

### <a name="64-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1108">6.4 一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1108">6.4 Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry Template</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1109">次要目錄專案的主要用途是提供目錄專案集的其他相關資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1109">The central purpose of secondary directory entries is to provide additional information about a directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1110">可解讀泛型次要 DirectoryEntry 範本的功能是必要的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1110">The ability to interpret the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template is mandatory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1111">重大和良性次要目錄專案的定義與次要 exFAT 修訂編號相關聯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1111">The definition of both critical and benign secondary directory entries correlates to the minor exFAT revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1112">此規格或後續規格的任何重大或良性次要目錄專案支援都是選擇性的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1112">Support for any critical or benign secondary directory entry this specification, or subsequent specifications, defines is optional.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1113">所有次要目錄專案結構都衍生自一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本 (請參閱 [表 18](#table-18-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)) ，其衍生自一般 DirectoryEntry 範本 (請參閱 [6.2 節](#62-generic-directoryentry-template)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1113">All secondary directory entry structures derive from the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Table 18](#table-18-generic-secondary-directoryentry-template)), which derives from the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2](#62-generic-directoryentry-template)).</span></span>

<td><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1140">此為必要欄位，而且 <a href="#644-datalength-field">區段 6.4.4</a> 會定義其內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1140">This field is mandatory and <a href="#644-datalength-field">Section 6.4.4</a> defines its contents.</span></span></td>
</tr>

</table>

#### <a name="641-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1141">6.4.1 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1141">6.4.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1142">>entrytype 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 [6.2.1 一節](#621-entrytype-field)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1142">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1](#621-entrytype-field))</span></span>

##### <a name="6411-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1143">6.4.1.1 TypeCode 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1143">6.4.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1144">TypeCode 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1.1) [一節](#6211-typecode-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1144">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.1](#6211-typecode-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="6412-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1145">6.4.1.2 TypeImportance 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1145">6.4.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1146">TypeImportance 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1.2) [一節](#6212-typeimportance-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1146">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.2](#6212-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

###### <a name="64121-critical-secondary-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1147">6.4.1.2.1 重要的次要目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1147">6.4.1.2.1 Critical Secondary Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1148">重要的次要目錄專案包含適當管理其包含目錄專案集的重要資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1148">Critical secondary directory entries contain information which is critical to the proper management of its containing directory entry set.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1149">雖然您可以選擇是否要對任何特定的重要次要目錄專案提供支援，但無法辨識的重要目錄專案會將整個目錄專案集轉譯為無法辨識的 (，而不是適用的目錄專案範本) 的定義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1149">While support for any specific critical secondary directory entry is optional, an unrecognized critical directory entry renders the entire directory entry set as unrecognized (beyond the definition of the applicable directory entry templates).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1150">但是，如果目錄專案集至少包含一個執行無法辨識的重要次要目錄專案，則此執行最多應該會解讀目錄專案集內目錄專案的範本，而不是與目錄專案 (集內任何目錄專案相關聯的資料，而不是與目錄專案集內任何目錄專案相關聯的資料，請參閱 [7.4 節](#74-file-directory-entry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1150">However, if a directory entry set contains at least one critical secondary directory entry which an implementation does not recognize, then the implementation shall at most interpret the templates of the directory entries in the directory entry set and not the data any allocation associated with any directory entry in the directory entry set contains (File directory entries are an exception, see [Section 7.4](#74-file-directory-entry)).</span></span>

###### <a name="64122-benign-secondary-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1151">6.4.1.2.2 良性次要目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1151">6.4.1.2.2 Benign Secondary Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1152">良性次要目錄專案包含額外的資訊，可能有助於管理其包含的目錄專案集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1152">Benign secondary directory entries contain additional information which may be useful for managing its containing directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1153">任何特定良性次要目錄專案的支援是選擇性的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1153">Support for any specific benign secondary directory entry is optional.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1154">無法辨識的良性次要目錄專案不會將整個目錄專案集轉譯為無法辨識。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1154">Unrecognized benign secondary directory entries do not render the entire directory entry set as unrecognized.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1155">執行可能會忽略它無法辨識的任何無害次要專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1155">Implementations may ignore any benign secondary entry it does not recognize.</span></span>

##### <a name="6413-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1156">6.4.1.3 TypeCategory 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1156">6.4.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1157">TypeCategory 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1.3) [一節](#6213-typecategory-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1157">The TypeCategory field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.3](#6213-typecategory-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1158">針對此範本，此欄位的有效值為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1158">For this template, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

##### <a name="6414-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1159">6.4.1.4 InUse 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1159">6.4.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1160">InUse 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.1.4) [一節](#6214-inuse-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1160">The InUse field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.1.4](#6214-inuse-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="6421-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1182">6.4.2.1 AllocationPossible 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1182">6.4.2.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

#### <a name="643-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1186">6.4.3 FirstCluster 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1186">6.4.3 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1187">FirstCluster 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.2.2) [一節](#622-firstcluster-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1187">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.2](#622-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1188">如果 NoFatChain 位為1，則 FirstCluster 必須指向叢集堆積中的有效群集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1188">If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then FirstCluster must point to a valid cluster in the cluster heap.</span></span>

#### <a name="644-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1189">6.4.4 DataLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1189">6.4.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1190">DataLength 欄位必須符合一般 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱上面 6.2.3) [一節](#623-datalength-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1190">The DataLength field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.2.3](#623-datalength-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1191">如果 NoFatChain 位為1，則 DataLength 不得為零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1191">If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then DataLength must not be zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1192">如果 FirstCluster 欄位為零，則 DataLength 也必須為零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1192">If the FirstCluster field is zero, then DataLength must also be zero.</span></span>

## <a name="7-directory-entry-definitions"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1193">7個目錄專案定義</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1193">7 Directory Entry Definitions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1194">ExFAT 檔案系統的修訂1.00 定義了下列目錄專案：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1194">Revision 1.00 of the exFAT file system defines the following directory entries:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1195">重大主要</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1195">Critical primary</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1196">配置點陣圖 ([區段 7.1](#71-allocation-bitmap-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1196">Allocation Bitmap ([Section 7.1](#71-allocation-bitmap-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1197">上案例資料表 ([區段 7.2](#72-up-case-table-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1197">Up-case Table ([Section 7.2](#72-up-case-table-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1198">磁片區標籤 ([區段 7.3](#73-volume-label-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1198">Volume Label ([Section 7.3](#73-volume-label-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1199">檔 ([區段 7.4](#74-file-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1199">File ([Section 7.4](#74-file-directory-entry))</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1200">無害的主要</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1200">Benign primary</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1201">磁片區 GUID ([區段 7.5](#75-volume-guid-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1201">Volume GUID ([Section 7.5](#75-volume-guid-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1202">TexFAT 填補 ([區段 7.10](#710-texfat-padding-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1202">TexFAT Padding ([Section 7.10](#710-texfat-padding-directory-entry))</span></span>

<!-- -->

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1203">重要次要</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1203">Critical secondary</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1204">資料流程延伸模組 ([區段 7.6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1204">Stream Extension ([Section 7.6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1205">檔案名 ([區段 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1205">File Name ([Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry))</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1206">良性次要</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1206">Benign secondary</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1207">廠商延伸模組 ([第7.8 節](#78-vendor-extension-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1207">Vendor Extension ([Section 7.8](#78-vendor-extension-directory-entry))</span></span>

  - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1208">廠商配置 ([區段 7.9](#79-vendor-allocation-directory-entry)) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1208">Vendor Allocation ([Section 7.9](#79-vendor-allocation-directory-entry))</span></span>

### <a name="71-allocation-bitmap-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1209">7.1 配置點陣圖目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1209">7.1 Allocation Bitmap Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1210">在 exFAT 檔案系統中，FAT 不會描述叢集的配置狀態;配置點陣圖則是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1210">In the exFAT file system, a FAT does not describe the allocation state of clusters; rather, an Allocation Bitmap does.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1211">配置點陣圖存在於叢集堆積中 (請參閱 [7.1.5) 一節](#715-allocation-bitmap) ，在根目錄中有對應的重要主要目錄專案 (請參閱 [表 20](#table-20-allocation-bitmap-directoryentry-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1211">Allocation Bitmaps exist in the Cluster Heap (see [Section 7.1.5](#715-allocation-bitmap)) and have corresponding critical primary directory entries in the root directory (see [Table 20](#table-20-allocation-bitmap-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1212">NumberOfFats 欄位會決定根目錄中有效配置點陣圖目錄專案的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1212">The NumberOfFats field determines the number of valid Allocation Bitmap directory entries in the root directory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1213">如果 NumberOfFats 欄位包含值1，則唯一有效的配置點陣圖目錄專案數目為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1213">If the NumberOfFats field contains the value 1, then the only valid number of Allocation Bitmap directory entries is 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1214">此外，只有在描述第一個配置點陣圖 (參閱 7.1.2.1) 一 [節](#7121-bitmapidentifier-field) 時，才會有一個配置點陣圖目錄專案是有效的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1214">Further, the one Allocation Bitmap directory entry is only valid if it describes the First Allocation Bitmap (see [Section 7.1.2.1](#7121-bitmapidentifier-field)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1215">如果 NumberOfFats 欄位包含值2，則唯一有效的配置點陣圖目錄專案數目是2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1215">If the NumberOfFats field contains the value 2, then the only valid number of Allocation Bitmap directory entries is 2.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1216">此外，兩個配置點陣圖目錄專案只有在描述第一個配置點陣圖時才有效，另一個則描述第二個配置點陣圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1216">Further, the two Allocation Bitmap directory entries are only valid if one describes the First Allocation Bitmap and the other describes the Second Allocation Bitmap.</span></span>

<div id="table-20-allocation-bitmap-directoryentry-structure" />

#### <a name="711-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1244">7.1.1 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1244">7.1.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1245">>entrytype 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.1) [一節](#631-entrytype-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1245">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1](#631-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7111-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1246">7.1.1.1 TypeCode 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1246">7.1.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1247">TypeCode 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.1.1) [一節](#6311-typecode-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1247">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.1](#6311-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1248">對於配置點陣圖目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1248">For an Allocation Bitmap directory entry, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

##### <a name="7112-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1249">7.1.1.2 TypeImportance 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1249">7.1.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

##### <a name="7121-bitmapidentifier-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1273">7.1.2.1 BitmapIdentifier 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1273">7.1.2.1 BitmapIdentifier Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1274">BitmapIdentifier 欄位應該會指出給定目錄專案所描述的配置點陣圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1274">The BitmapIdentifier field shall indicate which Allocation Bitmap the given directory entry describes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1275">「執行」應該使用第一個配置點陣圖搭配第一個 FAT，而且應該使用第二個配置點陣圖搭配第二個 FAT。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1275">Implementations shall use the First Allocation Bitmap in conjunction with the First FAT and shall use the Second Allocation Bitmap in conjunction with the Second FAT.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1276">ActiveFat 欄位說明哪些 FAT 和配置點陣圖為作用中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1276">The ActiveFat field describes which FAT and Allocation Bitmap are active.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1277">此欄位的有效值應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1277">The valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1278">0，表示指定的目錄專案會描述第一個配置點陣圖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1278">0, which means the given directory entry describes the First Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1279">1，表示指定的目錄專案會描述第二個配置點陣圖，而且只有在 NumberOfFats 包含值2時，才可能發生</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1279">1, which means the given directory entry describes the Second Allocation Bitmap and is possible only when NumberOfFats contains the value 2</span></span>

#### <a name="713-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1280">7.1.3 FirstCluster 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1280">7.1.3 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1281">FirstCluster 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.5) [一節](#635-firstcluster-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1281">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1282">此欄位包含叢集鏈第一個叢集的索引，如同 FAT 所述，它會裝載配置點陣圖。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1282">This field contains the index of the first cluster of the cluster chain, as the FAT describes, which hosts the Allocation Bitmap.</span></span>

#### <a name="714-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1283">7.1.4 DataLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1283">7.1.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1284">DataCluster 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.6) [一節](#636-datalength-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1284">The DataCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="715-allocation-bitmap"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1285">7.1.5 配置點陣圖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1285">7.1.5 Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1286">配置點陣圖會記錄叢集堆積中叢集的配置狀態。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1286">An Allocation Bitmap records the allocation state of the clusters in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1287">配置點陣圖中的每個位都會指出其對應的叢集是否可供配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1287">Each bit in an Allocation Bitmap indicates whether its corresponding cluster is available for allocation or not.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1288">配置點陣圖代表從最低到最高索引的叢集 (請參閱 [表 22](#table-22-allocation-bitmap-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1288">An Allocation Bitmap represents clusters from lowest to highest index (see [Table 22](#table-22-allocation-bitmap-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1289">基於歷史原因，第一個叢集的索引為2。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1289">For historical reasons, the first cluster has index 2.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1290">注意：點陣圖中的第一個位是第一個位元組的最低順序位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1290">Note: the first bit in the bitmap is the lowest-order bit of the first byte.</span></span>

##### <a name="7151-bitmapentry2--bitmapentryclustercount1-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1324">7.1.5.1 BitmapEntry \[ 2 \] .。。BitmapEntry \[ ClusterCount + 1 個 \] 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1324">7.1.5.1 BitmapEntry\[2\] ... BitmapEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1325">此陣列中的每個 BitmapEntry 欄位都代表叢集堆積中的叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1325">Each BitmapEntry field in this array represents a cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1326">BitmapEntry \[ 2 \] 代表叢集堆積中的第一個叢集，而 BitmapEntry \[ ClusterCount + 1 代表叢集中的 \] 最後一個叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1326">BitmapEntry\[2\] represents the first cluster in the Cluster Heap and BitmapEntry\[ClusterCount+1\] represents the last cluster in the Cluster Heap.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1327">這些欄位的有效值應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1327">The valid values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1328">0，描述可供配置的對應叢集</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1328">0, which describes the corresponding cluster as available for allocation</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1329">1，將對應的叢集描述為無法配置 (叢集配置可能已經取用對應的叢集，或使用中的 FAT 可能會將對應的叢集描述為錯誤) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1329">1, which describes the corresponding cluster as not available for allocation (a cluster allocation may already consume the corresponding cluster or the active FAT may describe the corresponding cluster as bad)</span></span>

### <a name="72-up-case-table-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1330">7.2 向上案例資料表目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1330">7.2 Up-case Table Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1331">Up 案例資料表定義從小寫轉換為大寫字元的轉換。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1331">The Up-case Table defines the conversion from lower-case to upper-case characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1332">這點很重要，因為檔案名目錄專案 (請參閱7.7 章節) 使用 Unicode 字元和 exFAT 檔案系統不區分大小寫，並保留大小寫。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1332">This is important due to the File Name directory entry (see Section 7.7) using Unicode characters and the exFAT file system being case insensitive and case preserving.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1333">此案例資料表存在於叢集堆積 (請參閱 7.2.5) [一節](#725-up-case-table) 中，並在根目錄中有對應的重要主要目錄專案 (請參閱 [表格 23](#table-23-up-case-table-directoryentry-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1333">The Up-case Table exists in the Cluster Heap (see [Section 7.2.5](#725-up-case-table)) and has a corresponding critical primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 23](#table-23-up-case-table-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1334">有效的 Up 案例資料表目錄專案數目為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1334">The valid number of Up-case Table directory entries is 1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1335">由於 Up 案例資料表和檔案名之間的關聯性，因此，除了格式作業的結果之外，實作為結果不應修改向上案例資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1335">Due to the relationship between the Up-case Table and file names, implementations should not modify the Up-case Table, except as a result of format operations.</span></span>

#### <a name="722-tablechecksum-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1379">7.2.2 TableChecksum 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1379">7.2.2 TableChecksum Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1380">[TableChecksum] 欄位包含 [FirstCluster] 和 [DataLength] 欄位描述) 的向上案例資料表 (總和檢查碼。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1380">The TableChecksum field contains the checksum of the Up-case Table (which the FirstCluster and DataLength fields describe).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1381">在使用向上案例資料表之前，必須先驗證此欄位的內容是否有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1381">Implementations shall verify the contents of this field are valid prior to using the Up-case Table.</span></span>

<div id="figure-3-tablechecksum-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1382">**圖 3 TableChecksum 計算**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1382">**Figure 3 TableChecksum Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt32 TableChecksum
(
    UCHAR  * Table,    // points to an in-memory copy of the up-case table
    UInt64   DataLength
)
{
    UInt32 Checksum = 0;
    UInt64 Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < DataLength; Index++)
    {
        Checksum = ((Checksum&1) ? 0x80000000 : 0) + (Checksum>>1) + (UInt32)Table[Index];
    }

    return Checksum;
}
```

#### <a name="723-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1383">7.2.3 FirstCluster 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1383">7.2.3 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1384">FirstCluster 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.5) [一節](#635-firstcluster-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1384">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.5](#635-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1385">此欄位包含叢集鏈第一個叢集的索引，如同 FAT 所述，它會裝載高案例資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1385">This field contains the index of the first cluster of the cluster chain, as the FAT describes, which hosts the Up-case Table.</span></span>

#### <a name="724-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1386">7.2.4 DataLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1386">7.2.4 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1387">DataCluster 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.6) [一節](#636-datalength-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1387">The DataCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.6](#636-datalength-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="725-up-case-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1388">7.2.5 Up-案例資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1388">7.2.5 Up-case Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1389">高案例資料表是一系列的 Unicode 字元對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1389">An up-case table is a series of Unicode character mappings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1390">字元對應是由2個位元組的欄位所組成，其中的 up 案例資料表中的欄位索引代表要加上大寫的 Unicode 字元，而2個位元組的欄位則代表大寫的 Unicode 字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1390">A character mapping consists of a 2-byte field, with the index of the field in the up-case table representing the Unicode character to be up-cased, and the 2-byte field representing the up-cased Unicode character.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1391">前128個 Unicode 字元具有強制對應 (請參閱 [表格 24](#table-24-mandatory-first-128-up-case-table-entries)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1391">The first 128 Unicode characters have mandatory mappings (see [Table 24](#table-24-mandatory-first-128-up-case-table-entries)).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1392">針對前128個 Unicode 字元，具有任何其他字元對應的 up 案例資料表無效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1392">An up-case table which has any other character mapping for any of the first 128 Unicode characters is invalid.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1393">僅支援強制對應範圍中之字元的實作為，可能會忽略下一個案例資料表其餘部分的對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1393">Implementations which only support characters from the mandatory mapping range may ignore the mappings of the rest of the up-case table.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1394">在透過檔案名目錄專案建立或重新命名 (檔案時，這類的執行應該只會使用強制對應範圍中的字元，請參閱 [7.7) 一節](#77-file-name-directory-entry) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1394">Such implementations shall only use characters from the mandatory mapping range when creating or renaming files (via the File Name directory entry, see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1395">當您的現有檔案名出現上限時，這類的執行不應該是從非強制對應範圍中的大寫字元，但應該在產生的大寫檔案名中保持不變， (這是部分的大小寫) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1395">When up-casing existing file names, such implementations shall not up-case characters from the non-mandatory mapping range, but shall leave them intact in the resulting up-cased file name (this is a partial up-casing).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1396">比較檔案名時，這類的執行應該會將與名稱不同的檔案名從非強制對應範圍中的 Unicode 字元視為相等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1396">When comparing file names, such implementations shall treat file names which differ from the name under comparison only by Unicode characters from the non-mandatory mapping range as equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1397">雖然這類檔案名只是可能對等的，但這類的執行無法確保完整大小寫的檔案名不會與下一個比較的名稱相衝突。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1397">While such file names are only potentially equivalent, such implementations cannot ensure the fully up-cased file name does not collide with the name under comparison.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1526">**0068h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1526">**0068h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1527">**0048h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1527">**0048h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1528">**0049h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1528">**0049h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1529">**004Ah**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1529">**004Ah**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1530">**004Bh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1530">**004Bh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1531">**004Ch**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1531">**004Ch**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1532">**004Dh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1532">**004Dh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1533">**004Eh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1533">**004Eh**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1534">**004Fh**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1534">**004Fh**</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1535">**0070h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1535">**0070h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1536">**0050h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1536">**0050h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1537">**0051h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1537">**0051h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1538">**0052h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1538">**0052h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1539">**0053h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1539">**0053h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1540">**0054h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1540">**0054h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1541">**0055h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1541">**0055h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1542">**0056h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1542">**0056h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1543">**0057h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1543">**0057h**</span></span> |
| <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1544">**0078h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1544">**0078h**</span></span>       | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1545">**0058h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1545">**0058h**</span></span>         | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1546">**0059h**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1546">**0059h**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1547">**005Ah**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1547">**005Ah**</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1548">007Bh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1548">007Bh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1549">007Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1549">007Ch</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1550">007Dh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1550">007Dh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1551">007Eh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1551">007Eh</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1552">007Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1552">007Fh</span></span>     |

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1553">**(附注：具有非身分識別的案例對應的專案會以粗體顯示)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1553">**(Note: entries with non-identity up-case mappings are in bold)**</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1554">格式化磁片區時，可能會使用身分識別對應壓縮來產生壓縮格式的高案例資料表，因為 Unicode 字元空間的其中一大部分並沒有案例的概念 (這表示「小寫」和「大寫」字元等同于) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1554">Upon formatting a volume, implementations may generate an up-case table in a compressed format using identity-mapping compression, since a large portion of the Unicode character space has no concept of case (which means the "lower-case" and "upper-case" characters are equivalent).</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1555">實值會藉由代表一系列的識別對應，並以 FFFFh 後面加上識別對應的數目，來壓縮高案例資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1555">Implementations compress an up-case table by representing a series of identity mappings with the value FFFFh followed with the number of identity mappings.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1556">例如，可能會使用下列八個壓縮的案例資料表專案，來表示 64h) 字元對應的前一個 100 (：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1556">For example, an implementation may represent the first 100 (64h) character mappings with the following eight entries of a compressed up-case table:</span></span>

> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1557">FFFFh, 0061h, 0041h, 0042h, 0043h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1557">FFFFh, 0061h, 0041h, 0042h, 0043h</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1558">前兩個專案表示前 97 (61h) 字元 (從0000h 到 0060h) 具有身分識別對應。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1558">The first two entries indicate the first 97 (61h) characters (from 0000h to 0060h) have identity mappings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1559">後續的字元（0061h 至0063h）會分別對應至0041h 至0043h 的字元。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1559">The subsequent characters, 0061h through 0063h, map to characters 0041h through 0043h, respectively.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1560">將磁片區格式化時提供壓縮的案例資料表的功能是選擇性的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1560">The ability to provide a compressed up-case table upon formatting a volume is optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1561">不過，您可以同時解讀未壓縮和壓縮的案例資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1561">However, the ability to interpret both an uncompressed and a compressed up-case table is mandatory.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1562">[TableChecksum] 欄位的值一律符合在磁片區上存在的案例資料表，可能是壓縮或未壓縮的格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1562">The value of the TableChecksum field always conforms to how the up-case table exists on the volume, which may be in either compressed or uncompressed format.</span></span>

##### <a name="7251-recommended-up-case-table"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1563">7.2.5.1 建議的 Up 案例資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1563">7.2.5.1 Recommended Up-case Table</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1564">格式化磁片區時，執行應以壓縮格式記錄建議的案例資料表 (請參閱 [ [表 25](#table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format) ]) ，其中 TableChecksum 欄位的值為 E619D30Dh。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1564">When formatting a volume, implementations should record the recommended up-case table in compressed format (see [Table 25](#table-25-recommended-up-case-table-in-compressed-format)), for which the value of the TableChecksum field is E619D30Dh.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-1565">如果實作為定義自己的案例資料表（壓縮或未壓縮），則該資料表應涵蓋完整的 Unicode 字元範圍 (從字元碼0000h 到 FFFFh 內含) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-1565">If an implementation defines its own up-case table, either compressed or uncompressed, then that table shall cover the complete Unicode character range (from character codes 0000h to FFFFh inclusive).</span></span>

### <a name="73-volume-label-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4860">7.3 磁片區標籤目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4860">7.3 Volume Label Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4861">磁片區標籤是 Unicode 字串，可讓使用者區別其存放磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4861">The Volume Label is a Unicode string which enables end users to distinguish their storage volumes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4862">在 exFAT 檔案系統中，磁片區標籤會以根目錄中的主要目錄專案形式存在， (請參閱 [表格 26](#table-26-volume-label-directoryentry-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4862">In the exFAT file system, the Volume Label exists as a critical primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 26](#table-26-volume-label-directoryentry-structure)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4863">有效的磁片區標籤目錄專案數目範圍從0到1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4863">The valid number of Volume Label directory entries ranges from 0 to 1.</span></span>

#### <a name="731-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4887">7.3.1 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4887">7.3.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4888">>entrytype 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.1) [一節](#631-entrytype-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4888">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1](#631-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7311-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4889">7.3.1.1 TypeCode 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4889">7.3.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4890">TypeCode 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.1.1) [一節](#6311-typecode-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4890">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.1](#6311-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4891">針對磁片區標籤目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4891">For the Volume Label directory entry, the valid value for this field is</span></span>
3.

##### <a name="7312-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4892">7.3.1.2 TypeImportance 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4892">7.3.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4893">TypeImportance 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.1.2) [一節](#6312-typeimportance-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4893">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.2](#6312-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4894">針對磁片區標籤目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4894">For the Volume Label directory entry, the valid value for this field is</span></span>
0.

##### <a name="7313-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4895">7.3.1.3 TypeCategory 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4895">7.3.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4896">TypeCategory 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.1.3) [一節](#6313-typecategory-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4896">The TypeCategory field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.3](#6313-typecategory-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7314-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4897">7.3.1.4 InUse 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4897">7.3.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4898">InUse 欄位必須符合一般主要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.3.1.4) [一節](#6314-inuse-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4898">The InUse field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Primary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.3.1.4](#6314-inuse-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="732-charactercount-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4899">7.3.2 CharacterCount 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4899">7.3.2 CharacterCount Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4900">CharacterCount 欄位必須包含 VolumeLabel 欄位包含的 Unicode 字串長度。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4900">The CharacterCount field shall contain the length of the Unicode string the VolumeLabel field contains.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4901">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4901">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4902">至少為0，這表示 Unicode 字串的長度為0個字元， (相當於無磁片區標籤) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4902">At least 0, which means the Unicode string is 0 characters long (which is the equivalent of no volume label)</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4903">最多11個，這表示 Unicode 字串長度為11個字元</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4903">At most 11, which means the Unicode string is 11 characters long</span></span>

#### <a name="733-volumelabel-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4904">7.3.3 VolumeLabel 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4904">7.3.3 VolumeLabel Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4905">VolumeLabel 欄位必須包含 Unicode 字串，也就是磁片區的使用者易記名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4905">The VolumeLabel field shall contain a Unicode string, which is the user-friendly name of the volume.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4906">VolumeLabel 欄位與檔案名目錄專案的 FileName 欄位有相同的無效字元組 (請參閱 [7.7.3) 一節](#773-filename-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4906">The VolumeLabel field has the same set of invalid characters as the FileName field of the File Name directory entry (see [Section 7.7.3](#773-filename-field)).</span></span>

### <a name="74-file-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4907">7.4 檔案目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4907">7.4 File Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4908">檔案目錄專案會描述檔案和目錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4908">File directory entries describe files and directories.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4909">它們是重要的主要目錄專案，任何目錄可能包含零或多個檔案目錄專案 (請參閱 [表格 27](#table-27-file-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4909">They are critical primary directory entries and any directory may contain zero or more File directory entries (see [Table 27](#table-27-file-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4910">若要讓檔案目錄專案有效，只有一個資料流程延伸目錄專案，而且至少一個檔案名目錄專案必須緊接在檔案目錄專案後面 (請分別參閱 [第7.6 節](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry) 和 [第7.7 節](#77-file-name-directory-entry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4910">For a File directory entry to be valid, exactly one Stream Extension directory entry and at least one File Name directory entry must immediately follow the File directory entry (see [Section 7.6](#76-stream-extension-directory-entry) and [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="741-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-4974">7.4.1 版 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-4974">7.4.1 EntryType Field</span></span>
