#### <a name="745-createtimestamp-create10msincrement-and-createutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5027">7.4.5 CreateTimestamp、Create10msIncrement 和 CreateUtcOffset 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5027">7.4.5 CreateTimestamp, Create10msIncrement, and CreateUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5028">CreateTimestamp 和 CreateTime10msIncrement 欄位組合時，會描述指定的檔案/目錄建立的本機日期和時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5028">In combination, the CreateTimestamp and CreateTime10msIncrement fields shall describe the local date and time the given file/directory was created.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5029">CreateUtcOffset 欄位描述當地日期和時間與 UTC 之間的時差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5029">The CreateUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5030">建立指定的目錄專案集時，應設定這些欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5030">Implementations shall set these fields upon creation of the given directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5031">這些欄位必須符合 Timestamp、10msIncrement 和 UtcOffset 欄位的定義 (請分別參閱7.4.8、[區段 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields)和[區段 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields)[一節](#748-timestamp-fields)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5031">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp, 10msIncrement, and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields), and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="746-lastmodifiedtimestamp-lastmodified10msincrement-and-lastmodifiedutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5032">7.4.6 LastModifiedTimestamp、LastModified10msIncrement 和 LastModifiedUtcOffset 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5032">7.4.6 LastModifiedTimestamp, LastModified10msIncrement, and LastModifiedUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5033">LastModifiedTimestamp 和 LastModifiedTime10msIncrement 欄位組合時，會描述與指定的資料流程延伸目錄專案相關聯之任何叢集的內容上次修改的本地日期和時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5033">In combination, the LastModifiedTimestamp and LastModifiedTime10msIncrement fields shall describe the local date and time the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry were last modified.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5034">LastModifiedUtcOffset 欄位描述當地日期和時間與 UTC 之間的時差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5034">The LastModifiedUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5035">實作為應更新這些欄位：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5035">Implementations shall update these fields:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5036">在修改任何與指定的資料流程延伸目錄專案相關聯之叢集的內容之後 (除了 ValidDataLength 欄位所描述的內容之外的內容之外) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5036">After modifying the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry (except for contents which exist beyond the point the ValidDataLength field describes)</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5037">變更 ValidDataLength 或 DataLength 欄位的值時</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5037">Upon changing the values of either the ValidDataLength or DataLength fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5038">這些欄位必須符合 Timestamp、10msIncrement 和 UtcOffset 欄位的定義 (請分別參閱7.4.8、[區段 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields)和[區段 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields)[一節](#748-timestamp-fields)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5038">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp, 10msIncrement, and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields), [Section 7.4.9](#749-10msincrement-fields), and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

#### <a name="747-lastaccessedtimestamp-and-lastaccessedutcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5039">7.4.7 LastAccessedTimestamp 和 LastAccessedUtcOffset 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5039">7.4.7 LastAccessedTimestamp and LastAccessedUtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5040">LastAccessedTimestamp 欄位應描述上次存取指定的資料流程延伸目錄專案之任何叢集內容的本地日期和時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5040">The LastAccessedTimestamp field shall describe the local date and time the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry were last accessed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5041">LastAccessedUtcOffset 欄位描述當地日期和時間與 UTC 之間的時差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5041">The LastAccessedUtcOffset field describes the offset of local date and time from UTC.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5042">實作為應更新這些欄位：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5042">Implementations shall update these fields:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5043">在修改任何與指定的資料流程延伸目錄專案相關聯之叢集的內容之後 (除了 ValidDataLength 以外的內容之外) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5043">After modifying the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry (except for contents which exist beyond the ValidDataLength)</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5044">變更 ValidDataLength 或 DataLength 欄位的值時</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5044">Upon changing the values of either the ValidDataLength or DataLength fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5045">在讀取任何與指定的資料流程延伸目錄專案相關聯的叢集內容之後，必須更新這些欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5045">Implementations should update these fields after reading the contents of any of the clusters associated with the given Stream Extension directory entry.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5046">這些欄位必須符合時間戳記和 UtcOffset 欄位的定義 (請) 分別參閱7.4.8 和[區段 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields)[一節](#748-timestamp-fields)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5046">These fields shall conform to the definitions of the Timestamp and UtcOffset fields (see [Section 7.4.8](#748-timestamp-fields) and [Section 7.4.10](#7410-utcoffset-fields), respectively).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5048">時間戳記欄位會以兩秒的解析度描述本機日期和時間 (請參閱 [資料表 29](#table-29-timestamp-field-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5048">Timestamp fields describe both local date and time, down to a two-second resolution (see [Table 29](#table-29-timestamp-field-structure)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7481-doubleseconds-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5080">7.4.8.1 DoubleSeconds 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5080">7.4.8.1 DoubleSeconds Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5081">DoubleSeconds 欄位應該會以兩秒的倍數描述時間戳記欄位的秒數部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5081">The DoubleSeconds field shall describe the seconds portion of the Timestamp field, in two-second multiples.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5082">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5082">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5083">0，代表0秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5083">0, which represents 0 seconds</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5084">29，代表58秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5084">29, which represents 58 seconds</span></span>

##### <a name="7482-minute-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5085">7.4.8.2 分鐘欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5085">7.4.8.2 Minute Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5086">[分鐘] 欄位應描述時間戳記欄位的分鐘部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5086">The Minute field shall describe the minutes portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5087">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5087">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5088">0，代表0分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5088">0, which represents 0 minutes</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5089">59，代表59分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5089">59, which represents 59 minutes</span></span>

##### <a name="7483-hour-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5090">7.4.8.3 Hour 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5090">7.4.8.3 Hour Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5091">[小時] 欄位應描述 [時間戳記] 欄位的小時部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5091">The Hour field shall describe the hours portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5092">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5092">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5093">0，表示00:00 小時</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5093">0, which represents 00:00 hours</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5094">23，代表23:00 小時</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5094">23, which represents 23:00 hours</span></span>

##### <a name="7484-day-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5095">7.4.8.4 Day 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5095">7.4.8.4 Day Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5096">Day 欄位必須描述時間戳記欄位的日部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5096">The Day field shall describe the day portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5097">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5097">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5098">1，這是指定月份的第一天</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5098">1, which is the first day of the given month</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5099">給定月份的最後一天 (指定的月份會定義有效的天數) </span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5099">The last day of the given month (the given month defines the number of valid days)</span></span>

##### <a name="7485-month-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5100">7.4.8.5 月份欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5100">7.4.8.5 Month Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5101">[月份] 欄位應描述 [時間戳記] 欄位的月份部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5101">The Month field shall describe the month portion of the Timestamp field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5102">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5102">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5103">至少1，代表1月</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5103">At least 1, which represents January</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5104">最多12個，表示12月</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5104">At most 12, which represents December</span></span>

##### <a name="7486-year-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5105">7.4.8.6 Year 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5105">7.4.8.6 Year Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5106">[年份] 欄位應描述時間戳記欄位的年份部分，相對於1980年。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5106">The Year field shall describe the year portion of the Timestamp field, relative to the year 1980.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5107">此欄位代表值為0且年份2107值為127的年份1980。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5107">This field represents the year 1980 with the value 0 and the year 2107 with the value 127.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5108">此欄位的所有可能值都是有效的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5108">All possible values for this field are valid.</span></span>

#### <a name="749-10msincrement-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5109">7.4.9 10msIncrement 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5109">7.4.9 10msIncrement Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5110">10msIncrement 欄位應該為其對應的時間戳記欄位提供10毫秒倍數的額外時間解析。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5110">10msIncrement fields shall provide additional time resolution to their corresponding Timestamp fields in ten-millisecond multiples.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5111">這些欄位之值的有效範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5111">The valid range of values for these fields shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5112">至少為0，表示0毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5112">At least 0, which represents 0 milliseconds</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5113">最多199，代表1990毫秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5113">At most 199, which represents 1990 milliseconds</span></span>

#### <a name="7410-utcoffset-fields"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5114">7.4.10 UtcOffset 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5114">7.4.10 UtcOffset Fields</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5115">UtcOffset 欄位 (請參閱 [表 30](#table-30-utcoffset-field-structure)) 描述從 UTC 到相對應的時間戳記和10msIncrement 欄位所述的當地日期和時間的位移。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5115">UtcOffset fields (see [Table 30](#table-30-utcoffset-field-structure)) shall describe the offset from UTC to the local date and time their corresponding Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields describe.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5116">UTC 與當地日期和時間之間的時差，包括時區和其他日期時間調整的效果，例如日光節約和區域夏季時間變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5116">The offset from UTC to the local date and time includes the effects of time zones and other date-time adjustments, such as daylight saving and regional summer time changes.</span></span>

##### <a name="74101-offsetfromutc-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5132">7.4.10.1 OffsetFromUtc 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5132">7.4.10.1 OffsetFromUtc Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5133">[OffsetFromUtc] 欄位描述的是與當地日期和時間相關的時間戳記與10msIncrement 欄位包含的 UTC 時差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5133">The OffsetFromUtc field shall describe the offset from UTC of the local date and time the related Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields contains.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5134">此欄位會以15分鐘的間隔描述 UTC 的位移 (請參閱表 31) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5134">This field describes the offset from UTC in 15 minute intervals (see Table 31).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5178">如上表所示，此欄位的所有可能值都是有效的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5178">As the table above indicates, all possible values for this field are valid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5179">不過，在下列情況下，執行應該只記錄這個欄位的00h 值：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5179">However, implementations should only record the value 00h for this field when:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5180">本機日期和時間實際上與 UTC 相同，在此情況下，OffsetValid 欄位的值應該是1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5180">Local date and time are actually the same as UTC, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 1</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5181">本機日期和時間是未知的，在此情況下，OffsetValid 欄位的值應該是1，而實值應將 UTC 視為當地日期和時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5181">Local date and time are not known, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 1 and implementations shall consider UTC to be local date and time</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5182">UTC 是未知的，在此情況下，OffsetValid 欄位的值應為0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5182">UTC is not known, in which case the value of the OffsetValid field shall be 0</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5183">如果當地日期和時間與 UTC 之間的時差不是15分鐘間隔的倍數，則在 OffsetFromUtc 欄位中的實作為「00h」就會記錄00h，並且應將 UTC 視為當地日期和時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5183">If the local date and time offset from UTC happens to not be a multiple of 15 minute intervals, then implementations shall record 00h in the OffsetFromUtc field and shall consider UTC to be local date and time.</span></span>

##### <a name="74102-offsetvalid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5184">7.4.10.2 OffsetValid 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5184">7.4.10.2 OffsetValid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5185">OffsetValid 欄位應描述 OffsetFromUtc 欄位的內容是否有效，如下所示：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5185">The OffsetValid field shall describe whether the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are valid or not, as follows:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5186">0，表示 OffsetFromUtc 欄位的內容無效</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5186">0, which means the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are invalid</span></span>
    > <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5187">和都必須是00h</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5187">and shall be 00h</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5188">1，表示 OffsetFromUtc 欄位的內容有效</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5188">1, which means the contents of the OffsetFromUtc field are valid</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5189">只有當 UTC 無法用於計算 OffsetFromUtc 欄位的值時，才應該將此欄位設定為值0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5189">Implementations should only set this field to the value 0 when UTC is not available for computing the value of the OffsetFromUtc field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5190">如果此欄位包含0這個值，則「實值」會將 Timestamp 和10msIncrement 欄位視為與目前本機日期和時間相同的 UTC 時差。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5190">If this field contains the value 0, then implementations shall treat the Timestamp and 10msIncrement fields as having the same UTC offset as the current local date and time.</span></span>

### <a name="75-volume-guid-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5191">7.5 磁片區 GUID 目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5191">7.5 Volume GUID Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5192">磁片區 GUID 目錄專案包含 GUID，可讓您以獨特的方式和程式設計方式區分磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5192">The Volume GUID directory entry contains a GUID which enables implementations to uniquely and programmatically distinguish volumes.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5193">磁片區 GUID 以良性的主要目錄專案的形式存在於根目錄中 (請參閱 [資料表 32](#table-32-volume-guid-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5193">The Volume GUID exists as a benign primary directory entry in the root directory (see [Table 32](#table-32-volume-guid-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5194">有效的磁片區 GUID 目錄專案數目範圍從0到1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5194">The valid number of Volume GUID directory entries ranges from 0 to 1.</span></span>

### <a name="76-stream-extension-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5253">7.6 資料流程延伸模組目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5253">7.6 Stream Extension Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5254">資料流程延伸目錄專案是檔案目錄專案集中的重要次要目錄專案 (請參閱 [資料表 33](#table-33-stream-extension-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5254">The Stream Extension directory entry is a critical secondary directory entry in File directory entry sets (see [Table 33](#table-33-stream-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5255">檔案目錄專案集中的資料流程延伸目錄專案有效位數為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5255">The valid number of Stream Extension directory entries in a File directory entry set is 1.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5256">此外，這個目錄專案只有在緊接在檔案目錄專案之後，才會是有效的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5256">Further, this directory entry is valid only if it immediately follows the File directory entry.</span></span>

#### <a name="763-namelength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5323">7.6.3 NameLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5323">7.6.3 NameLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5324">NameLength 欄位必須包含 Unicode 字串的長度，而後續的檔案名目錄專案 (請參閱) 統稱的 [第7.7 節](#77-file-name-directory-entry) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5324">The NameLength field shall contain the length of the Unicode string the subsequent File Name directory entries (see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)) collectively contain.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5325">此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5325">The valid range of values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5326">至少1，這是最短的可能檔案名</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5326">At least 1, which is the shortest possible file name</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5327">最長255，這是可能的最長檔名</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5327">At most 255, which is the longest possible file name</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5328">[NameLength] 欄位的值也會影響檔案名稱目錄專案 (請參閱 [7.7) 一節](#77-file-name-directory-entry) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5328">The value of the NameLength field also affects the number File Name Directory Entries (see [Section 7.7](#77-file-name-directory-entry)).</span></span>

#### <a name="764-namehash-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5329">7.6.4 NameHash 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5329">7.6.4 NameHash Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5330">NameHash 欄位必須包含2個位元組的雜湊 (請參閱 [ [圖 4](#figure-4-namehash-computation) ] 中的大寫檔案名的) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5330">The NameHash field shall contain a 2-byte hash (see [Figure 4](#figure-4-namehash-computation)) of the up-cased file name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5331">這可讓執行程式在依名稱搜尋檔案時執行快速比較。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5331">This enables implementations to perform a quick comparison when searching for a file by name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5332">重要的是，NameHash 會提供不相符的確認驗證。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5332">Importantly, the NameHash provides a sure verification of a mismatch.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5333">執行程式應使用最新的大小寫檔案名來確認所有 NameHash 相符專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5333">Implementations shall verify all NameHash matches with a comparison of the up-cased file name.</span></span>

<div id="figure-4-namehash-computation" />

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5334">**圖 4 NameHash 計算**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5334">**Figure 4 NameHash Computation**</span></span>

```C
UInt16 NameHash
(
    WCHAR * FileName,    // points to an in-memory copy of the up-cased file name
    UCHAR   NameLength
)
{
    UCHAR  * Buffer = (UCHAR *)FileName;
    UInt16   NumberOfBytes = (UInt16)NameLength * 2;
    UInt16   Hash = 0;
    UInt16   Index;

    for (Index = 0; Index < NumberOfBytes; Index++)
    {
        Hash = ((Hash&1) ? 0x8000 : 0) + (Hash>>1) + (UInt16)Buffer[Index];
    }
    return Hash;
}
```

#### <a name="765-validdatalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5335">7.6.5 ValidDataLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5335">7.6.5 ValidDataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5336">ValidDataLength 欄位應描述資料串流使用者資料的寫入時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5336">The ValidDataLength field shall describe how far into the data stream user data has been written.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5337">當您將資料寫入資料流程時，必須更新此欄位。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5337">Implementations shall update this field as they write data further out into the data stream.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5338">在儲存體媒體上，資料資料流程的有效資料長度與資料長度之間的資料是未定義的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5338">On the storage media, the data between the valid data length and the data length of the data stream is undefined.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5339">如果讀取作業的有效資料長度超過有效的長度，則實作為讀取作業的實作為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5339">Implementations shall return zeroes for read operations beyond the valid data length.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5340">如果對應的檔案目錄專案描述目錄，則此欄位唯一有效的值會等於 DataLength 欄位的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5340">If the corresponding File directory entry describes a directory, then the only valid value for this field is equal to the value of the DataLength field.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5341">否則，此欄位的有效值範圍應為：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5341">Otherwise, the range of valid values for this field shall be:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5342">至少為0，表示未將任何使用者資料寫入資料流程</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5342">At least 0, which means no user data has been written out to the data stream</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5343">最多 DataLength，這表示已將使用者資料寫出至整個資料流程長度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5343">At most DataLength, which means user data has been written out to the entire length of the data stream</span></span>

#### <a name="766-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5344">7.6.6 FirstCluster 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5344">7.6.6 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5345">FirstCluster 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.3) [一節](#643-firstcluster-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5345">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.3](#643-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5346">此欄位應該包含資料串流的第一個叢集的索引，其裝載使用者資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5346">This field shall contain the index of the first cluster of the data stream, which hosts the user data.</span></span>

#### <a name="767-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5347">7.6.7 DataLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5347">7.6.7 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5348">DataLength 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.4) [一節](#644-datalength-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5348">The DataLength field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.4](#644-datalength-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5349">如果對應的檔案目錄專案描述目錄，則此欄位的有效值為相關聯配置的整個大小（以位元組為單位），這可能是0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5349">If the corresponding File directory entry describes a directory, then the valid value for this field is the entire size of the associated allocation, in bytes, which may be 0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5350">此外，對於目錄而言，這個欄位的最大值是 256 MB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5350">Further, for directories, the maximum value for this field is 256MB.</span></span>

### <a name="77-file-name-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5351">7.7 檔案名目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5351">7.7 File Name Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5352">檔案名目錄專案是檔案目錄專案集中重要的次要目錄專案 (請參閱 [資料表 34](#table-34-file-name-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5352">File Name directory entries are critical secondary directory entries in File directory entry sets (see [Table 34](#table-34-file-name-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5353">檔案目錄專案集中檔案名目錄專案的有效數目為 NameLength/15，四捨五入到最接近的整數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5353">The valid number of File Name directory entries in a File directory entry set is NameLength / 15, rounded up to the nearest integer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5354">此外，只有在緊接以資料流程延伸目錄專案做為連續的系列時，才會將檔案名目錄專案視為有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5354">Further, File Name directory entries are valid only if they immediately follow the Stream Extension directory entry as a consecutive series.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5355">[檔案名] 目錄專案會合並以形成檔案目錄專案集的檔案名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5355">File Name directory entries combine to form the file name for the File directory entry set.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5356">給定目錄專案的所有子系都必須有唯一的檔案名目錄專案集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5356">All children of a given directory entry shall have unique File Name Directory Entry Sets.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5357">也就是說，在任何一個目錄內的大小寫之後，都不能有重複的檔案或目錄名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5357">That is to say there can be no duplicate file or directory names after up-casing within any one directory.</span></span>

#### <a name="771-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5377">7.7.1 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5377">7.7.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5378">>entrytype 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1) [一節](#641-entrytype-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5378">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1](#641-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7711-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5379">7.7.1.1 TypeCode 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5379">7.7.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5380">TypeCode 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1.1) [一節](#6411-typecode-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5380">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.1](#6411-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5381">若為數據流延伸目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5381">For the Stream Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

##### <a name="7712-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5382">7.7.1.2 TypeImportance 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5382">7.7.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5383">TypeImportance 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1.2) [一節](#6412-typeimportance-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5383">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.2](#6412-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5384">若為數據流延伸的目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5384">For the Stream Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7713-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5385">7.7.1.3 TypeCategory 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5385">7.7.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5386">TypeCategory 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1.3) [一節](#6413-typecategory-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5386">The TypeCategory field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.3](#6413-typecategory-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="772-generalsecondaryflags-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5389">7.7.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5389">7.7.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5390">GeneralSecondaryFlags 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱) [6.4.2 一節](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field) ，並定義要保留之 CustomDefined 欄位的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5390">The GeneralSecondaryFlags field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)) and defines the contents of the CustomDefined field to be reserved.</span></span>

##### <a name="7721-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5391">7.7.2.1 AllocationPossible 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5391">7.7.2.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5392">AllocationPossible 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.2.1) [一節](#6421-allocationpossible-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5392">The AllocationPossible field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.1](#6421-allocationpossible-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5393">若為數據流延伸的目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5393">For the Stream Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7722-nofatchain-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5394">7.7.2.2 NoFatChain 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5394">7.7.2.2 NoFatChain Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5395">NoFatChain 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.2.2) [一節](#6422-nofatchain-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5395">The NoFatChain field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="773-filename-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5396">7.7.3 FileName 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5396">7.7.3 FileName Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5397">FileName 欄位必須包含 Unicode 字串，這是檔案名的一部分。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5397">The FileName field shall contain a Unicode string, which is a portion of the file name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5398">在檔案目錄專案集的訂購檔案名目錄專案中，FileName 欄位會串連以形成檔案目錄專案集的檔案名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5398">In the order File Name directory entries exist in a File directory entry set, FileName fields concatenate to form the file name for the File directory entry set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5399">如果檔案名欄位的長度超過15個字元，且檔案名目錄專案的最大數目為17，則最後一個串連檔案名的長度上限為</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5399">Given the length of the FileName field, 15 characters, and the maximum number of File Name directory entries, 17, the maximum length of the final, concatenated file name is</span></span>
255.

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5400">串連的檔案名與其他 FAT 型檔案系統有同一組不合法的字元 (請參閱 [資料表 35](#table-35-invalid-filename-characters)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5400">The concatenated file name has the same set of illegal characters as other FAT-based file systems (see [Table 35](#table-35-invalid-filename-characters)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5401">實值應該將檔案名欄位的未使用字元設定為0000h 值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5401">Implementations should set the unused characters of FileName fields to the value 0000h.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5475">002Ah</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5475">002Ah</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5476">Asterisk</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5476">Asterisk</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5477">002Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5477">002Fh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5478">斜線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5478">Forward slash</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5479">003Ah</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5479">003Ah</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5480">冒號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5480">Colon</span></span>           |
| <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5481">003Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5481">003Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5482">小於符號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5482">Less-than sign</span></span>  | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5483">003Eh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5483">003Eh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5484">大於符號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5484">Greater-than sign</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5485">003Fh</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5485">003Fh</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5486">問號</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5486">Question mark</span></span>   |
| <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5487">005Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5487">005Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5488">反斜線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5488">Back slash</span></span>      | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5489">007Ch</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5489">007Ch</span></span>              | <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5490">直槓</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5490">Vertical bar</span></span>      |                    |                 |

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5491">檔案名 "." 和 "..." 分別具有「這個目錄」和「包含目錄」的特殊意義。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5491">The file names "." and ".." have the special meaning of "this directory" and "containing directory", respectively.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5492">在 [檔案名] 欄位中，「不應該」記錄這些保留的檔案名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5492">Implementations shall not record either of these reserved file names in the FileName field.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5493">但是，執行可能會在目錄清單中產生這兩個檔案名，以參考所列出的目錄和包含的目錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5493">However, implementations may generate these two file names in directory listings to refer to the directory being listed and the containing directory.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5494">執行可能會想要將檔案和目錄名稱限制為只有 ASCII 字元集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5494">Implementations may wish to restrict file and directory names to just the ASCII character set.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5495">如果有的話，它們應該將字元使用的字元限制為前128個 Unicode 專案中有效字元的範圍。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5495">If so they should limit their character use to the range of valid characters in the first 128 Unicode entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5496">它們仍然必須在磁片區上將檔案和目錄名稱儲存為 Unicode，並在與使用者互動時轉譯成 ASCII/Unicode。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5496">They must still store file and directory names in Unicode on the volume and translate to/from ASCII/Unicode when interfacing with the user.</span></span>

### <a name="78-vendor-extension-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5497">7.8 廠商延伸模組目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5497">7.8 Vendor Extension Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5498">廠商擴充功能目錄專案是檔案目錄專案集中的良性次要目錄專案 (請參閱 [資料表 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5498">The Vendor Extension directory entry is a benign secondary directory entry in File directory entry sets (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5499">檔案目錄專案集可包含任意數目的廠商擴充功能目錄專案，最多可達次要目錄專案的限制，而不是其他次要目錄專案的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5499">A File directory entry set may contain any number of Vendor Extension directory entries, up to the limit of secondary directory entries, less the number of other secondary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5500">此外，廠商延伸的目錄專案只有在不在必要的資料流程延伸模組和檔案名目錄專案之前，才有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5500">Further, Vendor Extension directory entries are valid only if they do not precede the required Stream Extension and File Name directory entries.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5501">廠商延伸目錄專案可讓廠商透過 VendorGuid 欄位，在個別的檔案目錄專案集中擁有唯一的廠商專屬目錄專案 (請參閱 [資料表 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5501">Vendor Extension directory entries enable vendors to have unique, vendor-specific directory entries in individual File directory entry sets via the VendorGuid field (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5502">唯一的目錄專案可以有效地讓供應商擴充 exFAT 檔案系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5502">Unique directory entries effectively enable vendors to extend the exFAT file system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5503">廠商可以定義 Vendordefined 向欄位的內容 (請參閱 [資料表 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5503">Vendors may define the contents of the VendorDefined field (see [Table 36](#table-36-vendor-extension-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5504">廠商的實施可能會維護 Vendordefined 向欄位的內容，並可提供廠商特有的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5504">Vendor implementations may maintain the contents of the VendorDefined field and may provide vendor-specific functionality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5505">無法辨識廠商延伸模組目錄專案的 GUID 的執行，應將目錄專案視為與任何其他無法辨識的良性次要目錄專案相同 (請參閱 [第8.2 節](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5505">Implementations which do not recognize the GUID of a Vendor Extension directory entry shall treat the directory entry the same as any other unrecognized benign secondary directory entry (see [Section 8.2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span></span>

#### <a name="781-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5529">7.8.1 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5529">7.8.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5530">>entrytype 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1) [一節](#641-entrytype-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5530">The EntryType field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1](#641-entrytype-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7811-typecode-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5531">7.8.1.1 TypeCode 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5531">7.8.1.1 TypeCode Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5532">TypeCode 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1.1) [一節](#6411-typecode-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5532">The TypeCode field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.1](#6411-typecode-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5533">針對廠商擴充功能目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5533">For the Vendor Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7812-typeimportance-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5534">7.8.1.2 TypeImportance 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5534">7.8.1.2 TypeImportance Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5535">TypeImportance 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1.2) [一節](#6412-typeimportance-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5535">The TypeImportance field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.2](#6412-typeimportance-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5536">針對廠商擴充功能目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5536">For the Vendor Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

##### <a name="7813-typecategory-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5537">7.8.1.3 TypeCategory 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5537">7.8.1.3 TypeCategory Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5538">TypeCategory 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1.3) [一節](#6413-typecategory-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5538">The TypeCategory field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.3](#6413-typecategory-field)).</span></span>

##### <a name="7814-inuse-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5539">7.8.1.4 版 InUse 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5539">7.8.1.4 InUse Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5540">InUse 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.1.4) [一節](#6414-inuse-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5540">The InUse field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.1.4](#6414-inuse-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="782-generalsecondaryflags-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5541">7.8.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5541">7.8.2 GeneralSecondaryFlags Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5542">GeneralSecondaryFlags 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱) [6.4.2 一節](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field) ，並定義要保留之 CustomDefined 欄位的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5542">The GeneralSecondaryFlags field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)) and defines the contents of the CustomDefined field to be reserved.</span></span>

##### <a name="7821-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5543">7.8.2.1 版 AllocationPossible 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5543">7.8.2.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5544">AllocationPossible 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.2.1) [一節](#6421-allocationpossible-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5544">The AllocationPossible field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.1](#6421-allocationpossible-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5545">針對廠商擴充功能目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為0。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5545">For the Vendor Extension directory entry, the valid value for this field is 0.</span></span>

##### <a name="7822-nofatchain-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5546">7.8.2.2 NoFatChain 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5546">7.8.2.2 NoFatChain Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5547">NoFatChain 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.2.2) [一節](#6422-nofatchain-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5547">The NoFatChain field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="783-vendorguid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5548">7.8.3 VendorGuid 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5548">7.8.3 VendorGuid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5549">VendorGuid 欄位必須包含可唯一識別指定廠商延伸模組的 GUID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5549">The VendorGuid field shall contain a GUID which uniquely identifies the given Vendor Extension.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5550">這個欄位的所有可能值都是有效的，但 null GUID 除外，也就是 {00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000} 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5550">All possible values for this field are valid, except the null GUID, which is {00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000}.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5551">不過，廠商應該使用 GUID 產生工具（例如 GuidGen.exe），在定義擴充功能時選取 GUID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5551">However, vendors should use a GUID-generating tool, such as GuidGen.exe, to select a GUID when defining their extensions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5552">此欄位的值會決定 Vendordefined 向欄位的供應商特定結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5552">The value of this field determines the vendor-specific structure of the VendorDefined field.</span></span>

### <a name="79-vendor-allocation-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5553">7.9 廠商配置目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5553">7.9 Vendor Allocation Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5554">廠商配置目錄專案是檔案目錄專案集中的良性次要目錄專案 (請參閱 [資料表 37](#table-37-vendor-allocation-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5554">The Vendor Allocation directory entry is a benign secondary directory entry in File directory entry sets (see [Table 37](#table-37-vendor-allocation-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5555">檔案目錄專案集可包含任意數目的廠商配置目錄專案，最多可達次要目錄專案的限制，而不是其他次要目錄專案的數目。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5555">A File directory entry set may contain any number of Vendor Allocation directory entries, up to the limit of secondary directory entries, less the number of other secondary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5556">此外，只有在所需的資料流程延伸模組和檔案名目錄專案之前，廠商配置目錄專案才會有效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5556">Further, Vendor Allocation directory entries are valid only if they do not precede the required Stream Extension and File Name directory entries.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5557">廠商配置目錄專案可讓廠商透過 VendorGuid 欄位，在個別的檔案目錄專案集中擁有唯一的廠商專屬目錄專案 (請參閱 [資料表 37](#table-37-vendor-allocation-directoryentry)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5557">Vendor Allocation directory entries enable vendors to have unique, vendor-specific directory entries in individual File directory entry sets via the VendorGuid field (see [Table 37](#table-37-vendor-allocation-directoryentry)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5558">唯一的目錄專案可以有效地讓供應商擴充 exFAT 檔案系統。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5558">Unique directory entries effectively enable vendors to extend the exFAT file system.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5559">廠商可以定義相關聯叢集的內容（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5559">Vendors may define the contents of the associated clusters, if any exist.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5560">廠商的實施可能會維護相關聯叢集的內容（如果有的話），並可提供廠商特有的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5560">Vendor implementations may maintain the contents of the associated clusters, if any, and may provide vendor-specific functionality.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5561">無法辨識供應商配置目錄專案之 GUID 的執行作業，應該將目錄專案視為與任何其他無法辨識的良性次要目錄專案相同 (請參閱 [8.2 節](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5561">Implementations which do not recognize the GUID of a Vendor Allocation directory entry shall treat the directory entry the same as any other unrecognized benign secondary directory entry (see [Section 8.2](#82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries)).</span></span>

#### <a name="791-entrytype-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5593">7.9.1 >entrytype 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5593">7.9.1 EntryType Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5597">針對廠商配置目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5597">For the Vendor Allocation directory entry, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5606">GeneralSecondaryFlags 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱) [6.4.2 一節](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field) ，並定義要保留之 CustomDefined 欄位的內容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5606">The GeneralSecondaryFlags field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2](#642-generalsecondaryflags-field)) and defines the contents of the CustomDefined field to be reserved.</span></span>

##### <a name="7921-allocationpossible-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5607">7.9.2.1 AllocationPossible 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5607">7.9.2.1 AllocationPossible Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5608">AllocationPossible 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.2.1) [一節](#6421-allocationpossible-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5608">The AllocationPossible field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.1](#6421-allocationpossible-field)).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5609">針對廠商配置目錄專案，此欄位的有效值為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5609">For the Vendor Allocation directory entry, the valid value for this field is 1.</span></span>

##### <a name="7922-nofatchain-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5610">7.9.2.2 NoFatChain 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5610">7.9.2.2 NoFatChain Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5611">NoFatChain 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.2.2) [一節](#6422-nofatchain-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5611">The NoFatChain field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.2.2](#6422-nofatchain-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="793-vendorguid-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5612">7.9.3 VendorGuid 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5612">7.9.3 VendorGuid Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5613">VendorGuid 欄位必須包含可唯一識別指定供應商配置的 GUID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5613">The VendorGuid field shall contain a GUID which uniquely identifies the given Vendor Allocation.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5614">這個欄位的所有可能值都是有效的，但 null GUID 除外，也就是 {00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000} 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5614">All possible values for this field are valid, except the null GUID, which is {00000000-0000-0000-0000-000000000000}.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5615">不過，廠商應該使用 GUID 產生工具（例如 GuidGen.exe），在定義擴充功能時選取 GUID。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5615">However, vendors should use a GUID-generating tool, such as GuidGen.exe, to select a GUID when defining their extensions.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5616">此欄位的值會決定相關聯之叢集內容的廠商特定結構（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5616">The value of this field determines the vendor-specific structure of the contents of the associated clusters, if any exist.</span></span>

#### <a name="794-firstcluster-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5617">7.9.4 FirstCluster 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5617">7.9.4 FirstCluster Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5618">FirstCluster 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.3) [一節](#643-firstcluster-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5618">The FirstCluster field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.3](#643-firstcluster-field)).</span></span>

#### <a name="795-datalength-field"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5619">7.9.5 DataLength 欄位</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5619">7.9.5 DataLength Field</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5620">DataLength 欄位必須符合一般次要 DirectoryEntry 範本中提供的定義 (請參閱 6.4.4) [一節](#644-datalength-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5620">The DataLength field shall conform to the definition provided in the Generic Secondary DirectoryEntry template (see [Section 6.4.4](#644-datalength-field)).</span></span>

### <a name="710-texfat-padding-directory-entry"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5621">7.10 TexFAT 填補目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5621">7.10 TexFAT Padding Directory Entry</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5622">此規格（exFAT 修訂1.00 檔案系統基本規格）不會定義 TexFAT 填補目錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5622">This specification, exFAT Revision 1.00 File System Basic Specification, does not define the TexFAT Padding directory entry.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5623">不過，其類型代碼是1，而其類型重要性為1。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5623">However, its type code is 1 and its type importance is 1.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5624">此規格的執行應該會將 TexFAT 填補目錄專案視為與任何其他無法辨識的良性主要目錄專案相同，因此，不應移動 TexFAT 填補目錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5624">Implementations of this specification shall treat TexFAT Padding directory entries the same as any other unrecognized benign primary directory entries, implementations shall not move TexFAT Padding directory entries.</span></span>

## <a name="8-implementation-notes"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5625">8個執行注意事項</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5625">8 Implementation Notes</span></span>

### <a name="81-recommended-write-ordering"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5626">8.1 建議的寫入順序</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5626">8.1 Recommended Write Ordering</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5627">實作為可確保磁片區盡可能具有復原能力，以及其他無法避免的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5627">Implementations should ensure the volume is as resilient as possible to power faults and other unavoidable failures.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5628">建立新的目錄專案或修改叢集配置時，通常應遵循下列撰寫順序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5628">When creating new directory entries or modifying cluster allocations, implementations should generally follow this writing order:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5629">將 VolumeDirty 欄位的值設定為1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5629">Set the value of the VolumeDirty field to 1</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5630">視需要更新作用中的 FAT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5630">Update the active FAT, if necessary</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5631">更新使用中配置點陣圖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5631">Update the active Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5632">視需要建立或更新目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5632">Create or update the directory entry, if necessary</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5633">如果第一個步驟之前的值為0，請清除 [VolumeDirty] 欄位的值為0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5633">Clear the value of the VolumeDirty field to 0, if its value prior to the first step was 0</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5634">刪除目錄專案或釋放叢集配置時，執行應遵循下列撰寫順序：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5634">When deleting directory entries or freeing cluster allocations, implementations should follow this writing order:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5635">將 VolumeDirty 欄位的值設定為1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5635">Set the value of the VolumeDirty field to 1</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5636">如有必要，請刪除或更新目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5636">Delete or update the directory entry, if necessary</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5637">視需要更新作用中的 FAT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5637">Update the active FAT, if necessary</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5638">更新使用中配置點陣圖</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5638">Update the active Allocation Bitmap</span></span>

5. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5639">如果第一個步驟之前的值為0，請清除 [VolumeDirty] 欄位的值為0</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5639">Clear the value of the VolumeDirty field to 0, if its value prior to the first step was 0</span></span>

### <a name="82-implications-of-unrecognized-directory-entries"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5640">8.2 無法辨識之目錄專案的含意</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5640">8.2 Implications of Unrecognized Directory Entries</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5641">相同主要修訂編號、1和次要修訂編號（大於0）的未來 exFAT 規格，可能會定義新的良性主要、重大次要和良性次要目錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5641">Future exFAT specifications of the same major revision number, 1, and minor revision number higher than 0, may define new benign primary, critical secondary, and benign secondary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5642">只有較高主要修訂編號的 exFAT 規格可以定義新的重要主要目錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5642">Only exFAT specifications of a higher major revision number may define new critical primary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5643">此規格的實作為 exFAT 修訂1.00 檔案系統基本規格，應該能夠掛接和存取任何主要修訂編號1和任何次要修訂編號的 exFAT 磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5643">Implementations of this specification, exFAT Revision 1.00 File System Basic Specification, should be able to mount and access any exFAT volume of major revision number 1 and any minor revision number.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5644">這會呈現可能會遇到無法辨識之目錄專案的情況。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5644">This presents scenarios in which an implementation may encounter directory entries which it does not recognize.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5645">以下說明這些案例的含意：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5645">The following describe implications of these scenarios:</span></span>

1. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5646">根目錄中有無法辨識的重要主要目錄專案會呈現不正確磁片區。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5646">The presence of unrecognized critical primary directory entries in the root directory renders the volume invalid.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5647">在任何非根目錄中，除了檔案目錄專案以外，任何重要的主要目錄專案都會呈現不正確裝載目錄。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5647">The presence of any critical primary directory entry, except File directory entries, in any non-root directory, renders the hosting directory invalid.</span></span>

2. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5648">執行不應修改無法辨識的良性主要目錄專案或其相關聯的叢集配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5648">Implementations shall not modify unrecognized benign primary directory entries or their associated cluster allocations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5649">不過，刪除目錄時，以及只有在刪除目錄時，執行應刪除無法辨識的良性主要目錄專案，並釋放所有相關聯的叢集配置（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5649">However, when deleting a directory, and only when deleting a directory, implementations shall delete unrecognized benign primary directory entries and free all associated cluster allocations, if any.</span></span>

3. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5650">執行不應修改無法辨認的重要次要目錄專案或其相關聯的叢集配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5650">Implementations shall not modify unrecognized critical secondary directory entries or their associated cluster allocations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5651">目錄專案集中有一或多個無法辨識的重要次要目錄專案，會轉譯整個目錄專案集無法辨識。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5651">The presence of one or more unrecognized critical secondary directory entries in a directory entry set renders the entire directory entry set unrecognized.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5652">當您刪除包含一或多個無法辨識的重要次要目錄專案的目錄專案集時，必須釋放與無法辨識的重要次要目錄專案相關聯的所有叢集配置（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5652">When deleting a directory entry set which contains one or more unrecognized critical secondary directory entries, implementations shall free all cluster allocations, if any, associated with unrecognized critical secondary directory entries.</span></span>
   <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5653">此外，如果目錄專案集描述目錄，則可能會執行下列動作：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5653">Further, if the directory entry set describes a directory, implementations may:</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5654">跨越目錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5654">Traverse into the directory</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5655">列舉其包含的目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5655">Enumerate the directory entries it contains</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5656">刪除包含的目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5656">Delete contained directory entries</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5657">將包含的目錄專案移至不同的目錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5657">Move contained directory entries to a different directory</span></span>

   <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5658">但是，執行不應：</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5658">However, implementations shall not:</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5659">修改內含的目錄專案（刪除除外），如所述</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5659">Modify contained directory entries, except delete, as noted</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5660">建立新的包含目錄專案</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5660">Create new contained directory entries</span></span>

   - <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5661">開啟包含的目錄專案（依所述的往返和列舉除外）</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5661">Open contained directory entries, except traverse and enumerate, as noted</span></span>

4. <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5662">執行不應修改無法辨識的良性次要目錄專案或其相關聯的叢集配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5662">Implementations shall not modify unrecognized benign secondary directory entries or their associated cluster allocations.</span></span>
   <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5663">實作為應忽略無法辨識的良性次要目錄專案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5663">Implementations should ignore unrecognized benign secondary directory entries.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5664">刪除目錄專案集時，必須釋放與無法辨識的良性次要目錄專案相關聯的所有叢集配置（如果有的話）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5664">When deleting a directory entry set, implementations shall free all cluster allocations, if any, associated with unrecognized benign secondary directory entries.</span></span>

## <a name="9-file-system-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5665">9檔案系統限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5665">9 File System Limits</span></span>

### <a name="91-sector-size-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5666">9.1 磁區大小限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5666">9.1 Sector Size Limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5667">BytesPerSectorShift 欄位會定義最低和最大磁區大小的限制 (評估為 **下限：512個位元組; 上限：4096個位元組**) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5667">The BytesPerSectorShift field defines the lower and upper sector size limits (which evaluates to **lower limit: 512 bytes; upper limit: 4,096 bytes**).</span></span>

### <a name="92-cluster-size-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5668">9.2 叢集大小限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5668">9.2 Cluster Size Limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5669">SectorsPerClusterShift 欄位會定義 (**下限：1個磁區; 上限： 25--BytesPerSectorShift 個磁區** 的下限和上限叢集大小限制，其會評估為 32mb) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5669">The SectorsPerClusterShift field defines the lower and upper cluster size limits (**lower limit: 1 sector; upper limit: 25 -- BytesPerSectorShift sectors**, which evaluates to 32MB).</span></span>

### <a name="93-cluster-heap-size-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5670">9.3 叢集堆積大小限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5670">9.3 Cluster Heap Size Limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5671">叢集堆積至少應包含足夠的空間來裝載下列基本檔案系統結構：根目錄、所有配置點陣圖和向上案例資料表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5671">The Cluster Heap shall contain at least enough space to host the following basic file system structures: the root directory, all Allocation Bitmaps, and the Up-case Table.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5672">較低的叢集堆積大小限制是位於叢集堆積中每個基本檔案系統結構的大小下限的函數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5672">The lower Cluster Heap size limit is a function of the lower size limit of each of the basic file system structures which reside in the Cluster Heap.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5673">即使有最小的可能叢集 (512 個位元組) ，每個基本檔案系統結構都不需要一個以上的叢集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5673">Even given the smallest possible cluster (512 bytes), each of the basic file system structures needs no more than one cluster.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5674">因此， **下限為： 2 + NumberOfFats** 叢集，根據 [NumberOfFats] 欄位的值，評估為3或4個群集。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5674">Therefore, the **lower limit is: 2 + NumberOfFats clusters**, which evaluates to either 3 or 4 clusters, depending on the value the NumberOfFats field.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5675">叢集堆積大小上限是最大可能的群集數目的簡單函式，ClusterCount 欄位會定義 (**上限： 2 <sup>32</sup>-11** 叢集) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5675">The upper Cluster Heap size limit is a simple function of the maximum possible number of clusters, which the ClusterCount field defines (**upper limit: 2<sup>32</sup>- 11 clusters**).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5676">無論叢集大小為何，這類叢集堆積都有足夠的空間可至少裝載基本檔案系統結構。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5676">Regardless of the cluster size, such a cluster heap has enough space to at least host the basic file system structures.</span></span>

### <a name="94-volume-size-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5677">9.4 磁片區大小限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5677">9.4 Volume Size Limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5678">VolumeLength 欄位會定義 (下限： **2 <sup>20</sup>/2 <sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>磁區**（評估為 1 mb）的下限和上限磁片區大小限制： **上限： 2 <sup>64</sup>-1 個磁區**，根據最大的磁區大小，評估為大約 64ZB) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5678">The VolumeLength field defines the lower and upper volume size limits (lower limit: **2 <sup>20</sup>/ 2 <sup>BytesPerSectorShift</sup>sectors**, which evaluates to 1MB; **upper limit: 2<sup>64</sup>- 1 sectors**, which, given the largest possible sector size, evaluates to approximately 64ZB).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5679">不過，此規格建議在叢集堆積中不超過2個<sup>24</sup>-2 的叢集 (請參閱 [3.1.9) 一節](#319-clustercount-field) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5679">However, this specification recommends no more than 2<sup>24</sup>- 2 clusters in the Cluster Heap (see [Section 3.1.9](#319-clustercount-field)).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5680">因此，磁片區的建議上限是： ClusterHeapOffset + (2<sup>24</sup>-2) \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5680">Therefore, the recommended upper limit of a volume is: ClusterHeapOffset + (2<sup>24</sup>- 2) \* 2<sup>SectorsPerClusterShift</sup>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5681">假設有最大的叢集大小、32MB 和假設 ClusterHeapOffset 是 96MB (足夠的空間供主要和備份開機區域使用，而且只有第一個 FAT) ，建議的磁片區上限會評估為大約512TB。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5681">Given the largest possible cluster size, 32MB, and assuming ClusterHeapOffset is 96MB (enough space for the Main and Backup Boot regions and only the First FAT), the recommended upper limit of a volume evaluates to approximately 512TB.</span></span>

### <a name="95-directory-size-limits"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5682">9.5 目錄大小限制</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5682">9.5 Directory Size Limits</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5683">資料流程延伸目錄專案的 DataLength 欄位會定義 (**下限：0位元組、上限： 256mb**) 的下限和上限目錄大小限制。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5683">The DataLength field of the Stream Extension directory entry defines the lower and upper directory size limits (**lower limit: 0 bytes; upper limit: 256MB**).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5684">這表示目錄最多可裝載8388608個目錄專案 (每個目錄專案都會耗用32個位元組) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5684">This means a directory may host up to 8,388,608 directory entries (each directory entry consumes 32 bytes).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5685">假設有最小的檔案目錄專案集（三個目錄專案），目錄最多可裝載2796202個檔案。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5685">Given the smallest possible File directory entry set, three directory entries, a directory may host up to 2,796,202 files.</span></span>

## <a name="10-appendix"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5686">10附錄</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5686">10 Appendix</span></span>

### <a name="101-globally-unique-identifiers-guids"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5687">10.1 (Guid) 全域唯一識別碼</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5687">10.1 Globally Unique Identifiers (GUIDs)</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5688">GUID 是全域唯一識別碼的 Microsoft 實作為。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5688">A GUID is the Microsoft implementation of a universally unique identifier.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5689">GUID 是128位值，其中包含8個十六進位數位的一個群組，後面接著三個4個十六進位數位的群組，後面接著一個12個十六進位數位（例如 {6B29FC40-CA47-1067-B31D-00DD010662DA}）， (參閱 [表 38](#table-38-guid-structure)) 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5689">A GUID is a 128-bit value consisting of one group of 8 hexadecimal digits, followed by three groups of 4 hexadecimal digits each, and followed by one group of 12 hexadecimal digits, for example {6B29FC40-CA47-1067-B31D-00DD010662DA}, (see [Table 38](#table-38-guid-structure)).</span></span>

<div id="table-38-guid-structure" />

### <a name="102-partition-tables"></a><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5741">10.2 資料分割資料表</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5741">10.2 Partition Tables</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5742">為了確保 exFAT 磁片區在一組廣泛使用案例中的互通性，執行程式應針對 MBR 分割區儲存體使用分割類型07h，並針對 GPT 分割儲存體使用分割 GUID {EBD0A0A2-B9E5-4433-87C0-68B6B72699C7}。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5742">To ensure interoperability of exFAT volumes in a broad set of usage scenarios, implementations should use partition type 07h for MBR partitioned storage and partition GUID {EBD0A0A2-B9E5-4433-87C0-68B6B72699C7} for GPT partitioned storage.</span></span>

<blockquote>
<p><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5795">修改了不正確的語句：「如果 DataLength 為零，並將 NoFatChain 設定為」區段6.3.5 中的「FirstCluster 欄位應為零，而設定為」。如果6.4.3 位為1，則 NoFatChain 必須指向叢集堆積中的有效叢集」，以說明如果已設定 FirstCluster 位，則必須有有效的配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5795">Amended incorrect statement: “FirstCluster Field shall be zero if the DataLength is zero and NoFatChain is set” in Section 6.3.5 and Section 6.4.3 to “If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then FirstCluster must point to a valid cluster in the cluster heap“ to clarify that there must be valid allocation if the NoFatChain bit is set.</span></span></p>
<p><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5796">已新增 "如果 NoFatChain 位為1，則 DataLength 不得為零。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5796">Added “If the NoFatChain bit is 1 then DataLength must not be zero.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5797">如果 FirstCluster 欄位為零，則 DataLength 也必須是零 "到區段6.3.6 和區段6.4.4，以說明如果設定 NoFatChain 位，必須有有效的配置。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5797">If the FirstCluster field is zero, then DataLength must also be zero” to Section 6.3.6 and Section 6.4.4 to clarify that there must be valid allocation if the NoFatChain bit is set.</span></span></p>
<p><span data-ttu-id="93dc1-5798">已將著作權聲明更新為2010</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="93dc1-5798">Updated copyright notice to 2010</span></span></p>
</blockquote></td>
</tr>
